- **Intrusive re-experiencing.** Peter narrates fragmentary memories of acts performed in his body that he did not perform — a sexual relationship with Anna Maria Marconi, the murder of the villain Massacre, the construction of Spider-Island fortifications, the founding of Parker Industries. The file should mark this as the closest analog in the canon to a sustained dissociative-identity violation, and the symptom profile post-arc (intrusive recall, identity destabilization, hypervigilance around restraint) is what the workup flags.
- **The Anna Maria relationship.** He maintains it. The file should note this carefully: confronted with a woman who fell in love with his body while another consciousness operated it, his response is to honor the relational debt and try to know her on his own terms. This is consistent with the hypertrophied conscience and inconsistent with any of the lower-prosocial differentials.
- **Parker Industries.** Octavius built him a multinational. The subject inherits it and tries to run it (*Amazing Spider-Man* Vol. 4, Slott, 2015–17). The file should mark the entire PI interval as a long, doomed experiment in occupying a stable, powerful, public-facing adult life that was never structured by his own pathology. He cannot sustain it. *Secret Empire* gives him the editorial pretext to destroy the company himself — he detonates it to deny Hydra the technology — and the file should mark the speed of the destruction and the affect with which he describes it ("it never really was mine") as diagnostic. Stable success is intolerable; the system finds a moral justification for its dismantlement.

## 7. The Late-Middle Configuration (post-PI through the late 2010s)

The subject returns to Queens, to freelance precarity, to a basement-tier apartment, to the *Bugle* in some form, to a renewed and now-friendly but unrekindled relationship with MJ. The file should mark this configuration as the system's homeostatic setpoint — the arrangement it returns to whenever destabilized in either direction, toward catastrophe or toward stability. Forest Hills, financial pressure, MJ at conversational distance, May alive, the mask on at night.

The pattern across this whole middle period — call it the thirty years from Gwen's death through the post-PI reset — is the workup's central claim made longitudinally visible: the subject is offered, repeatedly, the conditions of his own healing (the marriage, Horizon, PI, the Avengers, the teaching post, Anna Maria), and the system finds, each time, the mechanism of return. Sometimes the mechanism is editorial; behaviorally it is always the same. He cannot allow himself to be a man who got to keep things, because the foundational ledger has not been closed, and closing it would require accepting that Ben's death was not his to prevent — which would, in his internal accounting, dissolve the meaning of every act of heroism he has performed since.

The file should close this section on the observation that this is also why he is still functioning. The other comparable subjects — Stark, Richards, Banner — resolved the equivalent wounds, in their own ways, and the file shows each of them drifting ethically across the same decades. Peter does not drift. The wound is the anchor. The middle period is the demonstration that the wound, ruinous as it is to him personally, has held him to a moral line that nothing else in his life would have.

— END SECTION —


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# CHRONOLOGY IV — RECENT HISTORY & CURRENT STATE

*Subject: PARKER, Peter Benjamin. File segment covers the most recent operational era through present-day status. All inferences derived from the longitudinal behavioral record and continuous with the analytical workup.*

---

## 4.1 Entry Conditions: How the Subject Arrived at the Present

To understand where the subject is *now*, the file must first locate the entry conditions of the current era. The proximate antecedents are four:

**(a) The post-Superior reconstitution.** The subject reclaimed his own body following an extended period of consciousness-suppression by a hostile intelligence (Slott, *Superior Spider-Man* #1–31, into *Amazing Spider-Man* vol. 3 #1). The dossier flags this as the somatic-violation precedent for everything subsequent. The body he resumed occupying had been used to construct an enterprise (Parker Industries), a doctoral credential, a security infrastructure, and a set of intimate attachments (notably Anna Maria Marconi) that he himself had not built. He inherited a life-shaped object he did not authorize. The behavioral consequence — visible immediately in the early Slott vol. 3 issues and persisting through every subsequent arc — is a low-grade depersonalization toward his own circumstances: he treats his own apparent successes as provisional, foreign, not-quite-his. This is consistent with the post-traumatic identity destabilization noted at §3.

**(b) The Parker Industries collapse (Slott, "Threat Level: Red," *ASM* vol. 4 #794–796 / "Go Down Swinging," #797–801).** The subject built, then deliberately demolished, a global technology firm to deny its assets to Otto Octavius. He chose immolation of the corporate self over compromise — the operational signature is identical to every prior trade-self-for-other gesture in the file (see Analytical §1, "One More Day," Superior, the marriage). Post-collapse he returned to baseline economic precarity. This was, in the strict clinical sense, a relief: the unfamiliar prosperity was discharged, and the subject re-entered the failure-shaped social niche the foundational self-concept requires.

**(c) The Osborn-Goblin endgame (same arc).** Aunt May survived; Norman Osborn was decisively contained. The recurrent attachment-figure jeopardy that drives the subject's entire operational tempo was, briefly, resolved. The behavioral response to this rare condition of *no immediate loved-one threat* is itself diagnostic: the subject did not rest. He generated new precarities almost immediately — financial, residential, romantic — which is the self-sabotage signature documented across DeFalco, DeMatteis, and Slott.

**(d) The Spencer run reset and the Kindred arc (Spencer, *ASM* vol. 5 #1–74, 2018–2021).** Mary Jane returned to cohabitation. The relationship was rebuilt deliberately, slowly, with the subject conducting himself with markedly greater emotional disclosure than at any prior canonical point. The Kindred arc then weaponized the Harry/Osborn substrate against him — the resurfacing of Sin-Eater-era guilt, the literalized graveyard imagery, the centipede-mouth motif — which the file reads as Spencer externalizing the subject's interior grief structure into antagonist form. The subject endured it, did not break, did not abandon the relationship. This is the most positive datum in recent history and should not be understated: under conditions designed precisely to trigger his oldest wound, he sustained an attachment without rupturing it.

## 4.2 The Wells Era and the Paul Interval (*ASM* vol. 6, 2022–2024)

The current era opens with an off-page event — the so-called "eight-month gap" — engineered by Wells to insert a fresh wound the reader and the subject would have to excavate in parallel. The behavioral facts the file can confirm:

- The subject was, for a period, estranged from Mary Jane, who entered a relationship with one Paul Rabin and assumed maternal responsibility for two children (Eva and Telford) in another reality before returning to this one.
- The subject was estranged from Aunt May for cause not initially disclosed.
- The subject was estranged from the wider hero community, including the Fantastic Four — a near-unprecedented isolation pattern.
- Norman Osborn, "sin-cleansed," was operating as the subject's principal benefactor and ostensible ally.

The behavioral readout across this interval is consistent with every prior catastrophic-loss episode: the subject did not narrate the wound, he absorbed it. He resumed quipping at elevated frequency (per §3, the quip-density-correlates-with-distress signature), accepted Osborn's funding while displaying micro-tells of revulsion (the panel-level body language across the run — hunched shoulder under handshake, ¾-turn away during dialogue — is the somatic correlate of accepting help one cannot tolerate accepting), and re-occupied a cramped, substandard apartment whose squalor served the punitive self-concept.

The handling of MJ's quasi-parenthood of the Rabin children is the single most clinically revealing datum of the entire current era. The subject did *not* rage, did not contest, did not attempt to reclaim. He stepped aside. The file reads this as the attachment-system terror operating in its purest form: he believed, on the structural evidence available to him, that MJ was safer and better-served without him, and therefore self-removal was the correct moral act. This is the Uncle Ben template recoded for an intimate partner. The cost to him personally is registered across the run in three behavioral indices: weight loss (the wiry-depleted body image of §2 sharpened to gaunt), sleep collapse (multiple panel-sequences of swinging-while-microsleeping), and a measurable rise in tactical recklessness in combat encounters.

## 4.3 Current Domicile, Economic Status, and Daily Tempo

**Residence.** A walk-up apartment in a marginal-rent stratum of the outer boroughs, condition substandard. The subject has cycled through approximately a dozen residences across the post-Superior era; the consistent feature is *insufficiency* — undersized, undermaintained, with the window or rooftop access prioritized over any domestic amenity. The fridge contents are a chronic file-level signature: condiments, expired dairy, leftover takeout in unidentifiable containers, occasional bulk-purchased protein bars consumed pre-patrol. There is rarely a meal cooked on-site. The bed is unmade as standing condition; the costume is air-dried over furniture; the laptop is open and warm at most observed intervals.

**Employment.** Unstable. The subject has, across the current era, intermittently worked at Threats and Menaces (the Bugle's online successor under Robbie Robertson), accepted freelance photographic and engineering contracts, briefly held an adjunct position adjacent to ESU, and accepted, with documented internal distress, Osborn-funded research access. No income stream has exceeded six months of stability. The pattern is consistent with §3's "structural inability to allow stable success."

**Daily tempo.** Reconstructed from canonical scene-frequency: wake (or fail to sleep) between 0500 and 0700; coffee, no breakfast; review of overnight scanner intercepts and social-media threat-flag aggregators on a phone whose screen is cracked and has been cracked across multiple writers' runs; morning patrol or work obligation, frequently in conflict; midday missed lunch; afternoon work or lab; early-evening patrol that extends into night patrol that extends, on bad nights, into pre-dawn; return to apartment, costume off, immediate collapse or, more commonly, two to three hours of insomniac rumination at the kitchen table. Showering is irregular and post-patrol rather than morning-anchored. The phone is checked compulsively for May, MJ, the surrogate-daughter figures, and any breaking incident in his patrol radius — the spider-sense provides no relief here, because the spider-sense does not warn him about *them*.

## 4.4 The Attachment Field, Present Tense

**Mary Jane Watson.** Reconciliation has, as of latest canon, been initiated and is fragile. The subject is engaged in the most psychologically demanding behavior in his repertoire: receiving forgiveness for an action (the off-page secret-keeping driving the eight-month gap) he experienced as morally necessary. He has begun, tentatively, to disclose rather than absorb. The file logs this as developmentally significant but not stable; under sufficient stress the secret-keeping default is expected to re-engage.

**May Parker.** Living, recovered from prior intervals of estrangement, in regular phone contact. The phone calls follow a documented script: she opens with welfare inquiry, he deflects with a joke, she asks about MJ, he deflects with a joke, she does not ask about Spider-Man, he does not raise it, she says she loves him, he says he loves her, the call ends. The script has been stable for approximately a decade of in-universe time. The subject can no more change it than he can change the bridge.

**Felicia Hardy.** Friendly-adversarial equilibrium. She continues to function as the partner against whom the subject cannot make himself behave responsibly, which is precisely her ongoing appeal as a *non*-romantic figure — she absorbs the channel of his behavior he most fears in himself, and returns it to him as comedy.

**The surrogate-daughter complex.** Anna Maria Marconi (residual from the Superior period, now collegial-friendly), the various Mayday-equivalents across spider-multiverse encounters, and the post-*Spider-Verse* network of younger spider-totems (Miles Morales centrally, Anya Corazon, Cindy Moon, Gwen Stacy of Earth-65) collectively occupy this register. Toward Miles in particular the subject behaves with a tenderness and a pedagogical patience absent from every other relational register in the file. The protective intensity is total; the willingness to step back and let Miles fail-and-learn is, behaviorally, the single piece of evidence in the file that the subject has *learned* anything from the foundational Ben event other than guilt.

**Norman Osborn.** Active proximity, ostensibly reformed, treated by the subject with the wary politeness one reserves for a sleeping animal of known temperament. The subject does not believe the reform. The subject behaves as if he believes it because the cost of behaving otherwise is to relitigate Harry, Gwen, the bridge, the bell, and the laugh — and the subject's affect-regulation budget does not permit it.

**J. Jonah Jameson.** Stable warm-adversarial equilibrium, now layered with mutual disclosure (Jameson knows). The relationship functions, on the subject's side, as one of the very few socially-licensed channels for sustained verbal aggression and is therefore essential cardiovascular maintenance for the affect system.

## 4.5 Costume, Equipment, Operational Signature

The current suit is a return to classic palette and construction (red-and-blue, fabric and webbing, no Stark-engineered nanotech, no Parker Industries variants). This is meaningful. The subject has reverted to a kit he can fabricate himself, repair himself, and replace from materials available on a sub-minimum-wage income. The reversion correlates with the post-Parker-Industries collapse and reads as a deliberate refusal of dependency. Web-shooters are mechanical, of his own design, with two redundant cartridges per wrist and a documented habit of running out at the worst possible moment — a recurring narrative beat that is also a behavioral signature: the subject under-provisions when planning, because over-provisioning would presume the right to succeed.

Patrol pattern: documented preference for the Queensboro and Manhattan Bridge corridors, with notable avoidance of the George Washington Bridge — the avoidance has persisted across decades and survives every era's reset (see §4, "avoidance"). Swing-rhythm is improvisational rather than economized; he could move more efficiently and chooses not to, because the inefficient arc is the one in which his face is, as noted in §3, relaxed.

## 4.6 Combat Posture and Recent Injury Load

Engagement style has, across the current era, drifted measurably more aggressive. Hits absorbed per encounter are up; first-strike rates are up; the verbal output during combat is elevated above even his already-elevated baseline. The file reads this as the kinetic discharge channel compensating for the partial closure of the verbal-disclosure channel under reconciliation conditions with MJ — affect that previously found no outlet is finding the only outlet that asks no questions.

Documented injuries this era: stab wounds (multiple), gunshot graze (one confirmed, others probable and concealed from May and MJ), concussion sequence sufficient that any non-enhanced subject would be neurologically disabled, broken fingers (left hand, on at least three occasions, healed crooked), and a recurring lumbar issue from the Master Planner sequela compounded by the Superior body's training regimen, which Octavius had altered without Peter's neuromuscular memory adapting. He does not seek medical care. He sets bones against doorframes.

## 4.7 Internal State, Present

The subject is, as of latest canonical observation, functional, productive, materially impoverished, romantically tentative, professionally drifting, and morally coherent. The dysregulation core (§4) remains. The compensations (§3) remain. The trajectory across the most recent era is, against expectation, mildly positive on the developmental axis: he has demonstrated, with MJ, the capacity to absorb a wound and re-enter the attachment rather than rupture from it; with Miles, the capacity to mentor without colonizing; with Osborn, the capacity to tolerate the intolerable without breaking ethical posture. These are not cures. They are skills, painfully accreted, costly to deploy, and reversible under sufficient stress.

The single most reliable forward indicator is this: the subject will not stop. The patrol will continue tonight, in whatever weather, on whatever sleep, against whatever opposition, regardless of what was said on the phone with May and regardless of what was not yet said to MJ. The bell that rang in the basement workshop in 1962 has not stopped ringing. He has, however, learned — slowly, incompletely, and at a price the file should not minimize — to swing in rhythm with it rather than only away from it.

**Current status: ACTIVE. Operational. Monitored. Not at acute risk. Chronically loaded. Stable within his characteristic instability. The file remains open.**

— END SECTION 4 —


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — PARKER, PETER BENJAMIN

*UATU Dossier, Section III. Compiled from longitudinal observation; clinical inference per Chapman (2019) and adjunct sources cited in provenance log. Subject is a category-anomalous somatic case: a human body operating chronically beyond human tolerance, repaired by an enhanced regenerative substrate, but psychologically processed through an unenhanced and largely untreated mind.*

---

## 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE (PRE-BITE, AGE 0–15)

### 1.1 Birth and infancy

Subject was a low-to-normal-birthweight male infant, delivered without recorded complication. No documented prenatal exposures. Within months of birth, the catastrophic loss of both biological parents (Richard and Mary Parker) occurred under circumstances concealed from the child for the entirety of his developmental window. This is logged as a **medical** datum, not merely a biographical one: ambiguous early loss without consolidating narrative is a documented risk factor for later complex grief presentation, and the subject's lifelong somatized guilt response is consistent with a pre-verbal organism that registered abandonment without ever being given the vocabulary to discharge it.

### 1.2 Childhood somatic profile

Forest Hills pediatric record (inferred from canon depictions across Lee/Ditko and subsequent retrospective issues): chronically underweight for age, narrow frame, mild myopia corrected by horn-rimmed lenses from approximately age nine onward, no documented atopic disease, no asthma despite the visual coding of frailty. Reported susceptibility to colds and respiratory minor illness consistent with a child carrying chronic low-level anxious arousal — May Parker's documented over-feeding behavior (wheatcakes, second helpings) reads as a caregiver compensating for a child she perceived as not thriving.

Dental record: unremarkable; the subject is not depicted with significant orthodontic intervention, which combined with his economic background suggests untreated minor malocclusion.

### 1.3 Pubertal somatic history

The pre-bite Peter is depicted as physically late-developing — undermuscled, undersized relative to Flash Thompson cohort, no athletic participation, and demonstrably uncoordinated (the gym-class flashbacks across the Lee, DeMatteis, and Straczynski runs show consistent motor avoidance). This profile — small, smart, uncoordinated, glasses — is itself the somatic medium of the peer scapegoating documented elsewhere in this file. The body was a social liability before it became a tactical asset, and the subject's relationship to his own physicality has never fully recovered from this period; he experiences his enhanced body as borrowed equipment rather than as self.

### 1.4 Sensory baseline

Severe myopia, corrected. (This will become relevant: post-bite, the refractive error spontaneously resolves, and the discarding of the glasses in AF #15 is one of the cleanest somatic-psychological inflection points in the file — the subject literally sees clearly for the first time at the moment he ceases to be the person he was.)

---

## 2. THE INCIDENT (AF #15) AND ACUTE TRANSFORMATION

### 2.1 Mechanism

Subject was bitten on the dorsum of the hand by an arachnid acutely irradiated during a public-science demonstration. Acute systemic envenomation/transduction event: febrile prodrome (canon depicts vertigo, near-syncope upon exiting the demonstration hall), followed within hours by progressive somatic transformation. No medical attention was sought. **No medical attention has ever been sought for the bite itself, in sixty years of canon.** This is the index instance of a lifelong pattern: the subject does not present to clinical settings for his own body.

### 2.2 Phenotypic outcome

The transformation produced, with reasonable consistency across runs:

- **Musculoskeletal:** strength approximately ten to twenty tons under load (Slott, DeFalco, JMS variant depictions); muscle density and tendon insertion strength scaled correspondingly. Bone density elevated. Subject can absorb falls and impacts that would shatter unenhanced skeleton.
- **Neuromuscular:** reaction time at the millisecond order; agility, balance, and proprioception elevated to a regime in which conscious motor planning is largely bypassed.
- **Integumentary:** development of microscopic setae on palms, fingerpads, and soles enabling van der Waals adhesion to most surfaces. The setae are not visible to unaided observation but are histologically present; subject can disengage adhesion volitionally, an act of distributed micromotor control that he performs unconsciously hundreds of times daily.
- **Sensory:** the so-called **spider-sense** — a precognitive somatic alert presenting subjectively as a tingling at the base of the skull, scaling in intensity with threat magnitude and proximity. DeMatteis and Straczynski both depict it as a chronic low-grade background hum that never fully extinguishes. *Clinical translation: the subject lives inside a permanent threat-detection signal. The neurological substrate of generalized anxiety is, in his case, not merely psychological — it is wired into the same apparatus that keeps him alive.*
- **Metabolic:** baseline caloric requirement approximately doubled, with markedly accelerated wound healing and clearance of toxins, infectious agents, and ethanol.
- **Visual:** resolution of pre-existing myopia.

### 2.3 Psychological sequelae of the transformation itself

The subject has never grieved the body he lost. The pre-bite Peter — small, slow, mockable — was the self he had organized identity around, and the abrupt deletion of that self by exogenous biological event left him, within the same forty-eight hours, with no Uncle Ben and no familiar body. He responded by treating the new body as a tool rather than as a self, which is the somatic substrate of the bifurcated identity structure documented in Section IV. He inhabits the enhanced body with the affect of a man driving a borrowed car carefully.

---

## 3. TRAUMATIC INJURY LEDGER

A non-enhanced human with this injury history would be permanently disabled, institutionalized, or dead. The subject is none of these because of the enhanced healing substrate, but the *cumulative psychological loading* of repeatedly surviving what should kill him is itself a clinical variable rarely addressed in canon and central to this file.

### 3.1 Blunt-force and orthopedic

Cracked or fractured ribs are a near-weekly occurrence across the entire publication record and are documented explicitly in the Master Planner arc (ASM #31–33), the Kraven encounters, and consistently in the JMS, Slott, and Spencer runs. Concussion is similarly routine. Subject has been thrown through brick walls (multiple), automobile windshields (multiple), reinforced glass (multiple), and from heights including the upper structure of the Brooklyn Bridge (ASM #121, with surviving impact recorded against riverine surface in later variant retellings) and from skyscraper height in the Morlun encounters (JMS, "The Other"). Repeated craniocerebral trauma at this volume, in any other subject, would produce by middle age a measurable chronic traumatic encephalopathy. The enhanced substrate appears to clear sub-clinical neuronal damage; the *behavioral* signature of repeated head trauma — impulsivity escalation, mood lability, executive disinhibition — is absent, which is itself diagnostic of the regenerative ceiling.

### 3.2 Penetrating injury

- **Gunshot:** multiple. Definitive instance, ASM #538 (Civil War: The Initiative-era), shot during the rescue protecting May Parker — this single injury kinetically initiated the bargain with Mephisto and is therefore the wound with the highest downstream cost in the file.
- **Stabbing:** multiple. The Morlun arc (JMS) involves repeated impalement, including being skewered through the torso; the "Spider-Wound" sequence depicts injuries clinically incompatible with non-enhanced survival.
- **Mauling/clawing:** multiple, primarily Lizard, Vulture, Black Cat (consensual, see §6), and the Kraven family arcs.

### 3.3 Thermal and chemical

Severe burns from incendiary/explosive devices (Hobgoblin pumpkin bombs; Green Goblin armaments), including partial-thickness burns to face, hands, and back across multiple incidents. Inhalational exposures to undocumented agents: Mysterio's hallucinogens (repeated, with documented dissociative aftereffect — see §7), Scorpion's pheromonal/chemical traces, multiple Lizard serum aerosols, the "Queen" pheromone exposure (Grim Hunt prequel arcs), and the Spider-Island viral exposure (Slott, 2011) in which subject was atypically asymptomatic owing to baseline arachnid loading. Lifetime exposure to undocumented industrial and exotic chemistry is in the 95th-plus percentile for any human subject; long-term oncological risk is unquantifiable.

### 3.4 Radiological

Baseline radiological loading from the index transformation event. Subsequent re-exposures (Doc Ock's labs, Octavius-era nuclear-handling sequences, multiple cosmic-radiation encounters during Avengers and Fantastic Four team-ups). The "Captain Universe" episode and subsequent cosmic-tier engagements have exposed the subject to energetic loadings without any conventional medical follow-up.

### 3.5 Clinical death events

The subject has clinically died at minimum twice in primary canon: (a) the "Other" arc (Hudson Street/JMS-era), in which death precedes a literal somatic moult and re-emergence with altered features, and (b) the Superior arc terminus (Slott), in which the subject's consciousness was suppressed and restored after demonstrable cessation of his somatic agency. Each death event is unprocessed; he has not, across canon, sat with a clinician and integrated the fact that he has died. Subjects who survive near-death events without integration carry elevated rates of intrusive re-experiencing, depersonalization, and altered death-anxiety profiles; the subject manifests all three, masked by humor.

### 3.6 Skeletal-muscular wear

Despite enhanced healing, the cumulative micro-trauma of swinging — repeated maximal-load shoulder rotations, wrist extension under tensile load, ankle and knee impact from rooftop landings — produces a chronic somatic substrate of low-grade musculoskeletal soreness that no writer has ever depicted as absent. He hurts, always, somewhere.

---

## 4. SLEEP

Chronic, severe, structurally enforced sleep restriction. Across writers (Conway, DeFalco, DeMatteis, JMS, Slott, Spencer, Wells), Peter is depicted operating routinely on two-to-four hours per night, frequently zero across multi-day operations. This is not lifestyle preference; it is the geometry of holding two full-time identities (employment, schooling, or research; and nightly patrol) inside a 24-hour cycle.

Clinical consequences:
- Documented micro-sleep episodes mid-conversation (DeMatteis "Spectacular" run).
- Cognitive lapses he attributes to "Parker Luck" but which are mechanistically attributable to executive function degradation under sleep debt.
- Mood lability amplification: the depressive collapses (post-Kraven, post-Superior) are temporally correlated with extended sleep deprivation preceding them.
- Driving and operational micro-errors masked by enhanced reflexes.
- The chronic spider-sense activation prevents deep sleep architecture; subject likely does not enter consolidated slow-wave sleep at population norms. **The threat-detection apparatus does not switch off, which means the recovery apparatus never fully switches on.**

He has never been formally assessed for sleep pathology. He would meet criteria for chronic insomnia with circadian disruption and probable REM-rebound abnormality.

---

## 5. NUTRITION AND METABOLIC STATE

Caloric requirement approximately twice unenhanced human baseline. Income across canon: chronically insufficient (Bugle freelance, adjunct teaching, Horizon Labs employment as the rare interval of stability, Parker Industries collapse, post-Parker-Industries return to precarity). The intersection of doubled requirement and chronic underemployment produces functional undernutrition across long stretches of his adult life.

Visual canon corroborates: wiry, vascular, low body-fat habitus rather than the hypertrophic build the strength figures would predict in a well-fed enhanced subject. Aunt May's persistent food-pushing behavior across decades reads, in light of this, as a caregiver who has never stopped seeing him as the underweight child of 1962; her instinct is correct, even though her stated reasons are not.

Hydration: poor; subject is depicted drinking coffee compulsively and water rarely. Caffeine intake is high and is among the few exogenous substances he uses for direct neuro-regulation.

---

## 6. SEXUAL AND REPRODUCTIVE HEALTH

Sexual history is monogamous-serial with a small number of intense partners (Betty Brant, Gwen Stacy, Mary Jane Watson, Felicia Hardy, Carlie Cooper, post-reset Mary Jane again). Reproductive: the May "Mayday" Parker continuity establishes biological fertility; the in-utero loss in the Clone Saga (the daughter ostensibly stillborn under Osborn's manipulation) is an unprocessed grief event that surfaces episodically in subsequent runs and is one of the cleanest examples in the file of an injury he carries without language.

The Felicia Hardy involvement is specifically a sexual pattern of interest: rooftop/danger-context intimacy, costume-on, identity-bracketed. The clinical read — danger-coupled sexual behavior in a subject with affect dysregulation and self-damaging coloring (Chapman 2019) — is direct: arousal coupled to threat is, for this subject, a regulatory mechanism, and the relationship with Felicia is the clearest behavioral instance.

No documented STI history; the enhanced immune substrate likely confers protective coverage that the subject has never empirically tested and should not assume.

---

## 7. SOMATIC VIOLATIONS AND IDENTITY-DESTABILIZING EVENTS

These are catalogued as **medical** because they were violations of bodily integrity with measurable psychiatric sequelae.

### 7.1 The Captain Universe episode

Possession of subject's body by the Uni-Power for an extended interval (Acts of Vengeance era). Subject emerged with no sustained physical alteration but with a temporary expanded perceptual loading he describes ambivalently across subsequent appearances.

### 7.2 The Other / spider-totem moult

The "Other" sequence (JMS et al., 2005–06) involved clinical death, somatic moult, and re-emergence with minor additional capacities (organic web variants, night-vision adaptation, retractable wrist stingers in some depictions). The transformation was unsought, was experienced as bodily horror, and was treated in canon as resolved when it was, behaviorally, not. Subsequent runs depict ongoing subtle dysmorphia: the subject does not trust his own body's stability after this event.

### 7.3 The Superior body-theft

Octavius's consciousness occupied subject's body for an extended period (Slott, 2012–14). Subject's awareness was, by varying accounts, suppressed or fragmentarily present. **This is the single most severe medical event in the file and is almost universally underrated as such.** The clinical analog is a prolonged dissociative violation in which the subject was a passive witness to acts performed by his own body — including sexual acts with Anna Maria Marconi, surgical and tactical decisions, and the public alteration of his social and professional identity. Post-restoration symptomatology (Slott's "Goblin Nation" aftermath into Spencer's run) includes:
- Intrusive re-experiencing of Octavius's perspective;
- Difficulty trusting his own intentions ("Was that me or him?");
- Specifically guilt-laden interactions with Anna Maria, mediated by the awareness that the relationship was initiated under a consent defect for which there is no clean remediation;
- Hyper-monitoring of his own behavior for evidence of contamination.

This is, in any standard clinical frame, complex post-traumatic stress with dissociative features layered on a pre-existing trauma architecture. He has not been clinically treated for it.

### 7.4 Spider-Island

Brief loss of unique-identity status (entire NYC population temporarily acquired his abilities, Slott 2011); resolved without lasting somatic effect but with documented narcissistic-injury overtones — the one thing that distinguished him from everyone else was, briefly, common property, and he was visibly distressed by this in a way that contradicts his stated self-concept.

### 7.5 Cosmic and dimensional displacement

Multiple Web of Life and Destiny / Spider-Verse exposures (Slott, Spencer) with unquantified neurological loading. The cumulative effect of repeated dimensional shears on a single nervous system is unstudied.

---

## 8. SUBSTANCES

**Alcohol:** Minimal. Subject drinks socially in limited quantity. The enhanced metabolism clears ethanol so rapidly that intoxication is functionally unattainable through ordinary intake — a fact he has tested only rarely. Notably, the subject does not pursue intoxication despite this freedom; the absence is itself diagnostic.

**Recreational drugs:** Absent. This is a deliberate authorial line from Stan Lee onward, set against Harry Osborn's pill arc (ASM #96–98), and it has held across six decades. The subject's abstinence in the face of an affective load that would predict heavy self-medication is the *single most diagnostically interesting datum in the substance category*: it indicates that his existing behavioral repertoire — humor, motion, work — is functioning as the medication, with enough efficacy that pharmacological supplementation has not been recruited. If those channels were blocked — sustained injury preventing patrol, sustained isolation preventing humor's audience, sustained unemployment preventing work — the substance-use risk profile would shift sharply.

**Caffeine:** High. Functional dependence.

**Tobacco:** Absent.

**Prescription medication:** Effectively none. Subject has not maintained continuous primary-care relationship and is not prescribed routine medication. No psychiatric medication has ever been trialled. *He has never been offered an SSRI; he has never refused one; he has simply never been asked.*

**Performance-enhancing or exotic:** The Captain Universe possession, the various radiation exposures, the totemic enhancements, and the brief "Iron Spider" technological augmentation under Stark all constitute exogenous somatic interventions of varying consent quality. None monitored.

---

## 9. SURGICAL HISTORY

Effectively none in conventional clinical settings. The subject has been sutured, set, and patched by:
- Himself (most commonly; bathroom mirror, dental floss in early canon, surgical thread later);
- Mary Jane Watson (extensive, across the marriage years; she developed competence at field-grade wound care);
- Aunt May (limited, under the cover story of "bicycle accidents," with a willing suspension of disbelief that itself merits clinical comment);
- The Black Cat (rooftop suturing depicted episodically);
- Curt Connors and, separately, Reed Richards and Tony Stark (in higher-acuity events);
- Night Nurse / Linda Carter network (Daredevil-adjacent informal medical infrastructure).

The cumulative scar load is substantial but partially remodeled by enhanced healing — visible scarring is patchy rather than disfiguring, but a full-body examination would reveal a topology of past wounds inconsistent with any non-combatant history.

---

## 10. THE SPIDER-SENSE AS CHRONIC NEUROLOGICAL CONDITION

This warrants its own subsection because no clinician in canon has ever framed it correctly. The spider-sense is, from the subject's phenomenological standpoint, *a never-silent low-grade alarm in his own skull*. It scales with threat, but it is never zero. The neurological cost of living inside a permanent threat-detection signal is the autonomic substrate of generalized anxiety — elevated baseline sympathetic tone, impaired parasympathetic recovery, sleep architecture disruption, and a startle threshold permanently calibrated for combat rather than civilian life.

When the spider-sense has been temporarily lost (multiple arcs, including Spencer's "Sins Rising" prelude and the Superior-era confusion), subject reports experience the loss as **relief** before they report it as vulnerability. This is the clearest somatic evidence that the apparatus that keeps him alive is also the apparatus that prevents him from resting.

---

## 11. GERIATRIC AND MORTALITY PROJECTION

Subject has not, in primary continuity, aged at expected human rate; publication convention holds him in extended young adulthood. Alternate-continuity futures (MC2, "Old Man" variants, Renew Your Vows) depict him aging into a recognizable late-middle-aged human with cumulative injury sequelae becoming more visible — limp, residual orthopedic dysfunction, slowed reflex, but cognition intact and conscience undimmed.

The actuarial expectation, given injury rate and the suppressive effect of the enhanced substrate on cumulative damage, is that he will outlive non-enhanced cohort norms *if and only if* an acute event does not kill him first. The acute risk is the dominant variable; cumulative risk is, paradoxically, low.

---

## 12. PSYCHOLOGICAL IMPACT — SYNTHESIS

The medical file's central finding is this: **the subject's body has been the primary site of his moral life.** He has experienced his strength as debt, his speed as obligation, his healing as license to absorb damage that protects others, and his constant low-grade pain as the appropriate cost of a power he did not earn. He does not seek medical care because medical care would treat his body as a thing worth preserving for its own sake, and that is a frame he does not hold about himself.

The somatic-violation events (Other, Superior, Spider-Island) compound on a pre-existing self-concept in which his body was always already not-quite-his — first because it was the wrong, weak body of pre-bite Peter, then because it was the borrowed, enhanced body that arrived the same week Uncle Ben left, then because it has been literally taken from him by other consciousnesses and returned with their fingerprints on it.

The absence of substance use, the absence of clinical contact, the absence of psychiatric medication, and the presence of one of the heaviest cumulative injury loads in any documented subject, together, describe a man who is treating himself the way he believes he deserves to be treated. The clinical task, if one were ever undertaken, would not begin with the injuries. It would begin with the question of why he has never asked anyone to look at them.

— END SECTION III —


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: PARKER, PETER BENJAMIN

*Longitudinal body-record. Compiled from direct observational data, recovered photographs, surveillance footage (rooftop and street-level), medical imaging where obtainable, and cross-referenced behavioral canon. All readings are calibrated to the subject's enhanced baseline; "elevated" and "depressed" are relative to that baseline, not to general population norms.*

---

## I. BUILD, FRAME, AND BASELINE MORPHOLOGY

The subject presents at approximately 5'10" and a fluctuating 165–180 lb, with the fluctuation tracking weeks of caloric sufficiency versus deficit rather than training cycles. The musculature is anomalous on imaging: lean mass density is roughly twice expected for the apparent cross-section, with disproportionate development in the posterior chain, the forearm flexors, the lumbricals, and the small intrinsic muscles of the hands and feet. The shoulder girdle is overdeveloped relative to the chest; the trapezius is hypertrophied bilaterally and slightly asymmetric (right > left, consistent with web-shooter recoil load). The hip flexors are short — a chronic shortening from years spent in apex-predator crouch.

Skin: pale beneath the mask-line, sun-exposed only on the lower face and hands. Numerous fine scars distributed across torso and limbs that should not be there given his regenerative profile — meaning the wounds that left them were severe enough to outpace healing. A particularly dense scar field across the lower right ribcage (the Morlun cluster) and along the left flank (the ASM #538 sniper wound). The dorsum of both hands shows micro-scarring at the wrist crease from years of web-shooter chafing. The fingertips and toe-pads, on dermatoscopic examination, are densely populated with the setal microstructures — invisible to gross observation but palpable as a faint, dry tackiness on contact.

Hair: brown, fine, perennially in need of a cut by two to three weeks. He cuts it himself, badly, in front of the bathroom mirror at intervals correlated with rent-due weeks (an avoidance behavior: barbers cost money and require sitting still while a stranger handles his head). Stubble appears within twelve hours of shaving and is patchy on the right jaw from an old scar he does not remember acquiring.

---

## II. FACE — MICRO-EXPRESSIVE INVENTORY

The unmasked face is more legible than the subject realizes. The default neutral is *not* neutral: a faint downward lateral pull of the lip corners, a habitual tension in the corrugator that produces a vertical micro-furrow between the brows even at rest. He is, at baseline, mildly braced.

**The smile** has three distinct forms, separable on slow-motion review.
- The *social compliance smile*: tight, symmetrical, no orbicularis involvement, deployed on demand for civilians, employers, landlords. Duration 0.4–0.8 seconds.
- The *genuine smile*, rare: asymmetric, slightly higher on the left, with full eye-crinkle and a brief head-tilt to the right. Triggered reliably by MJ, by May, by Johnny Storm's stupidity, by an elegant equation, and by a small subset of his own jokes that surprise him.
- The *under-the-mask grin*, inferable from voice modulation and chin position when masked: this is the broadest expression in his repertoire and exists almost exclusively in costume. The face he cannot show is the face he most freely makes.

**The eyebrows** are the single most diagnostic feature when unmasked. The left brow elevates independently — a habitual gesture of incredulity, deployed both at villains' monologues and at Aunt May's casserole proposals. Under genuine alarm, both brows pull together and down, the corrugator fires hard, and a transient asymmetry appears at the inner brow heads.

**The eyes** track at unusual speed; saccadic frequency is elevated, and surveillance footage in crowds shows him visually checking exit routes, overhead structures, and high windows at a rate of roughly one full sweep per twelve to fifteen seconds even in ostensibly safe environments. He makes solid eye contact in one-on-one conversation, but it is *too solid*; he forgets to break it at conventional intervals because he is monitoring the interlocutor's micro-expression for threat or disappointment rather than performing social rapport. Pupillary response to startle is suppressed below human norm — the spider-sense provides the alert before the optic pathway, and the gross startle reflex has been damped over years of constant low-grade activation.

**The mouth** is the loudest part of him. He licks his lower lip before speaking when nervous; he runs his tongue along the inner cheek when thinking; he chews the inside of the left cheek when ruminating, and there is a small chronic ulcer there visible on intraoral inspection. The jaw clenches at sleep — masseter hypertrophy is mild but present, and his molars show flat-wear consistent with bruxism.

---

## III. GAIT, POSTURE, AND AMBULATION

**Walking gait, civilian mode.** He has trained himself, with imperfect success, to walk like a slightly clumsy young man. The performance includes a deliberate looseness in the shoulders, a tendency to bump into door frames, and a stride length pulled in by roughly two inches from his natural range. The performance breaks under cognitive load: when distracted (running late, working a problem), the *actual* gait emerges — preternaturally smooth weight transfer, near-silent foot strike, a center of mass held lower than expected, and an unconscious tendency to take stairs three at a time on the way up. Trained observers (Murdock, Romanoff, Cage) have all identified him by gait alone within seconds.

**Standing posture.** Slightly forward-leaning at the hips, shoulders rolled inward. This is partly the lifelong scholar's posture and partly a deliberate self-minimization — he occupies less space than his frame would suggest. When he forgets, the posture corrects upward: spine lengthens, shoulders square, chin lifts. The corrected posture is what villains see immediately before he engages.

**Crouch.** His resting *combat* posture is a low predator crouch — knees deeply bent, weight on the forefoot, one hand often touching the surface for sensory input. He is comfortable in this position for hours; he reads in it, he eats in it on rooftops, he sleeps in it occasionally when injured and unwilling to lie supine. The posture is so habitual that civilians who encounter him in costume often describe the silhouette before they describe the colors.

**Sitting.** Cannot sit conventionally for long. In chairs, he migrates within ten minutes — one foot tucked under, then both, then a knee up against the chest. He reverses chairs to sit backward when distracted. In Aunt May's kitchen, surveillance shows him reverting to a contained, polite seated posture, hands folded — a regressed adolescent body-language consistent with that environment.

**Climbing.** Unconscious. He has been observed multiple times entering his own apartment via the wall when his keys were misplaced, with no apparent awareness that he had done so. The adhesion is volitional but the *choice* to climb has migrated below conscious threshold over the years.

---

## IV. HANDS — TICS, GESTURES, AND MICROSIGNATURES

The hands are the most expressive and most surveillable part of the subject.

The dominant manual gesture is a *pre-shooting flex*: the middle and ring fingers curl toward the palm while the index and pinky extend. He does this when anxious without ever firing webs — phantom mechanical action. It increases in frequency with stress and is visible across decades of footage, both masked and unmasked.

When thinking, he taps the pad of the thumb sequentially against the pads of the four fingers, distal to proximal, in a rolling cycle. Speed correlates with cognitive load. Under deep concentration the cycle is so fast it blurs.

When seated near food and not yet eating, he reorganizes objects — salt shaker, napkin, fork — into orthogonal alignments. The behavior is not commented on by intimates because it is so constant.

He picks at the cuticles of the left thumb when guilty. This produces a chronic small abrasion that never quite heals on the same calendar as the surrounding tissue, and surveillance can timestamp guilt periods by the state of that thumb.

He runs his palm over the back of his neck when caught in a lie or asked about his whereabouts. The gesture has been so reliable across so many years that MJ ceased asking direct questions and began watching the hand instead.

He wipes his palms on his thighs before any cognitively demanding social entry (job interviews, awkward dates, Jameson's office) regardless of whether the palms are sweating, which they rarely are.

In sleep, the hands curl into a half-fist with the index finger extended along the bedding — a residual web-shooter ready position.

---

## V. VOCAL PATTERN AND VERBAL TICS

The unmasked voice is a light tenor, faster than median speech rate (approximately 175 wpm at baseline, climbing to 220+ under stress), with a New York–outer-borough vowel set that thickens markedly in May's house and almost vanishes in academic settings (code-switching is unconscious and instantaneous).

The masked voice is lower by perhaps a quarter-octave and approximately 15% louder — a deliberate construction maintained for so long it has become natural under the hood. The cadence is also altered: shorter sentences, more rhythmically pointed, with the characteristic prosodic structure of the joke (setup-beat-punch) imposed even on tactical communication.

Verbal tics:
- *"Uh"* as a default opener, deployed to buy 200–400 milliseconds of cognitive runway.
- *"Look —"* as a transition to seriousness; he is about to either lie or tell an uncomfortable truth.
- A reliable habit of answering questions about himself with a question back, or with a deflective compliment to the asker.
- Under threat: the quip density increases inversely to his actual confidence. Silent-Spider-Man is the dangerous Spider-Man; chatty Spider-Man is the frightened one. This inversion has been noted by adversaries who have learned to read it (Octavius explicitly; the Kingpin operationally).
- He hums under his breath while working — typically fragments of whatever his uncle used to whistle, which he himself cannot consciously identify as Ben's repertoire.
- He laughs at his own jokes, briefly and quietly, often *before* delivering them — a tell.

---

## VI. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Chronically disrupted. Total sleep time averages 3.5–5 hours per 24-hour cycle, polyphasic by necessity rather than choice. Sleep onset is rapid (under four minutes) when the body crashes, but is preceded by extended periods of failure to *initiate* sleep — he will be horizontal but cognitively rehearsing the day's failures for thirty to ninety minutes.

REM density appears elevated on the rare occasions monitored; he dreams vividly and reports remembering them, which is itself a marker of fragmented sleep. Recurrent dream contents documented across multiple writers' canonical depictions: the bridge (Gwen), the warehouse (Ben), being underground (Kraven), being unable to lift something heavy off someone he loves (Master Planner template). These recur in clusters around anniversaries and stressors.

Sleep position: lateral right, knees drawn up, dominant arm under the pillow with the hand near the face. He startles awake at any auditory anomaly below 40 dB, including the building's elevator, before falling back asleep within seconds. He has been observed by intimates to twitch in his sleep at a rate consistent with periodic limb movements — the body firing micro-combat responses to dream stimuli. He talks in his sleep occasionally; the content is fragmentary, mostly names, mostly female (MJ, Gwen, May), with an occasional "Ben — wait."

Naps: takes them on rooftops, on the Bugle's break-room couch, in subway seats, in his lab chair. Twenty-minute units, eyes open within the first second of being addressed.

---

## VII. EATING AND NUTRITIONAL BEHAVIOR

Caloric requirement is approximately 4,500–6,000 kcal/day. He routinely fails to meet this. Eating behavior:

- *Speed*: very fast. He clears a plate in under five minutes and is often visibly still hungry afterward.
- *Bias toward portable, dense, cheap*: hot dogs, pizza by the slice, bodega sandwiches, peanut butter direct from the jar, cereal as a meal at any hour. A chronic Chinese-takeout container population in the refrigerator.
- *Coffee*: heavy, black, no longer affecting him meaningfully because of enhanced metabolism, but consumed ritually in volumes of 4–6 cups/day. The ritual matters more than the caffeine.
- *In May's house*: eats whatever she serves with performed enthusiasm, including the legendary wheatcakes and other questionable casseroles. Will accept seconds even when not hungry, because refusal injures her.
- *In MJ's presence*: eats more, more slowly, more variably. She is the only person who reliably *feeds* him, and his body responds to her cooking as a regulating ritual rather than a fuel intake.
- *Under acute stress*: forgets to eat entirely for 24–36 hour periods, then crashes catastrophically and overconsumes.
- *Post-fight*: shaking hands, low blood sugar, ravenous; the post-combat hot dog or bodega slice is so consistent across canon it constitutes a behavioral signature.

Hydration: inadequate. He drinks coffee, tap water from the bathroom sink, and whatever is in the fridge.

---

## VIII. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

The pattern with intimates is bimodal: prolonged emotional restraint punctuated by sudden, urgent physical closeness — typically initiated by him in the aftermath of near-death (a near-universal tell, identified by both Felicia Hardy and MJ across canon). This is the danger-sex pattern: post-adrenergic discharge channeled into intimacy as both regulation and reassurance-seeking.

With MJ: physical ease is high; he sleeps better in her bed than anywhere else (measurably so — the only sustained eight-hour sleep blocks in the record occur there). Touch is constant and small — hand on her wrist, palm at her lower back, forehead-to-forehead before parting. He kisses with eyes closed and a brief sharp inhale, a habit she has remarked on.

With Felicia: physical compatibility was extreme and emotionally destabilizing for him. The pattern was rooftop-encounters, mask partially on, identity protected — a configuration that suited her costume-fetishization and *also* his abandonment defense (less of himself disclosed, less to lose). He left those encounters more agitated than satisfied.

With Gwen, in the historical record: tender, awkward, mostly chaste in depiction, with a great deal of hand-holding and forehead-touching. The closest he came in those years to performed normalcy.

The general signature: he initiates touch in private and accepts it in public but does not initiate it in public. He flinches faintly at unexpected contact from strangers — a fraction of a second of full-body tension that he covers with a smile. He cannot tolerate being held down even playfully; partners learn this quickly.

---

## IX. THREAT-STATE SOMATICS

When the spider-sense activates, the body cascade is consistent and trackable:

1. *Sub-100 millisecond*: an involuntary minute lift of the chin and slight widening of the eyes; the head orients toward the threat vector before conscious awareness reports it.
2. *Within 200 ms*: weight transfers to the balls of the feet; the dominant hand drops a few inches toward the wrist of the other (pre-shooting position).
3. *Within 500 ms*: shoulders drop and roll forward; breathing shifts to a deeper, slower diaphragmatic rhythm — *paradoxical* to expectation, this is a trained response, the autonomic system having learned over years that hyperventilation degrades combat performance.
4. *Verbal*: a joke arrives within 1–2 seconds of threat recognition. Almost always.
5. *Post-engagement*: a hand-tremor that he conceals by stuffing the hand in a pocket or gripping something. Lasts 30–90 seconds. The civilians he just saved do not see it.

Under restraint or immobilization (the one condition his defenses cannot accommodate): rapid escalation. Breathing accelerates, jaw locks, pupils dilate; the quipping fragments and is replaced by silence, then by labored verbal aggression. This is the state in which he most closely resembles a panic attack, and it is the state villains who know him best engineer deliberately.

---

## X. GROOMING, DRESS, AND PERSONAL MAINTENANCE

Civilian dress is functional, cheap, layered. Brown leather jacket (multiple generations across decades, replaced only when destroyed). Button-down over T-shirt is a habitual configuration because it accommodates the suit underneath. Sneakers, worn through at the toe within weeks. Glasses occasionally as a deliberate identity-disguise (post-bite, his vision corrected, but the affectation is retained intermittently).

He showers in under four minutes — a New York economy and a habit. He brushes his teeth standing in the kitchen, walking, or while reading. He shaves irregularly; he forgets to until the stubble itches. He carries no wallet half the time, no keys often (he doesn't always need them).

His apartment, on every available depiction, is *organized chaos*: lab equipment and notebooks in rigid geometric order; everything domestic in entropy. The pattern is diagnostic — the parts of his life that serve the mission are disciplined; the parts that serve himself are neglected.

---

## XI. STATE-DEPENDENT MODULATION SUMMARY

- **Calm/safe** (rare; documented only in MJ's presence, in May's kitchen, in the lab mid-problem): face softens at the corrugator; the under-brow vertical furrow disappears; shoulders drop; the saccadic exit-scanning slows to roughly one sweep per minute; the hands still.
- **Working/intellectual flow**: the tongue moves along the inner cheek; the thumb-finger cycling accelerates; humming begins; ambient awareness drops below normal human levels (he can be approached unheard, a fact that startles him into apologies).
- **Social-performance mode**: the compliance smile; the deliberate stumble in gait; the self-deprecating opener; the palm-on-thigh wipe.
- **Stress, sub-acute**: missed meals; the cuticle picking; the neck-rub; sleep collapse; increased quip volume; cancellations.
- **Stress, acute**: the diaphragmatic breath; the crouch; the joke; the conserved-energy stillness between actions.
- **Post-combat**: tremor; hunger; the need for either MJ-presence or a rooftop alone for ten to fifteen minutes; an unwillingness to be touched by strangers (paramedics, journalists) immediately afterward.
- **Grief-state**: profound stillness — unusual for him. The verbal output drops to near zero. He sits, often outdoors, often at altitude, often facing east, for hours.
- **Intimacy**: slowed cadence, eye-contact softened rather than fixed, the small constant touches, the audible exhale on contact. The only state in which the body sets down its constant readiness, and even then, incompletely.

— END SOMATIC ATLAS —


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## SUBJECT: PARKER, PETER BENJAMIN

*File section 7 of 14. Cross-reference: §3 (Psychological), §4 (Psychiatric), §9 (Known Associates), §11 (Sexual & Romantic History).*

---

## 7.1 — Attachment Architecture: The Foundational Strata

The subject's attachment system was assembled in three discrete strata, each laid down before he had cognitive tools to inspect it, and each producing a measurable behavioral signature still observable in current relational conduct.

**Stratum I — The infant loss (age 0–4, pre-memory).** Richard and Mary Parker disappear from his life before any retrievable narrative memory can form. What is encoded instead is the somatic and procedural memory of attachment figures vanishing without explanation, followed by transfer to substitute caregivers (May and Ben Parker, Forest Hills). The cognitive content of this loss is unavailable to the subject; the procedural template is not. He behaves, across sixty years of canon, as if attachment is intrinsically interruptible — as if the *normal* outcome of loving someone is that they will be removed without notice and without his consent. This is observable in the micro-behavior of his goodbyes: across the Lee, Romita, DeFalco, JMS, and Slott runs, when leaving May or MJ for routine errands, the subject consistently performs a check-back glance at the doorway, a touch to the shoulder, a "love you" that no equivalent unmarked person would emit at that frequency. He is, behaviorally, never leaving anyone for the last time without having marked it.

**Stratum II — The fragile-caregiver household.** May Parker's chronic anxiety and somatic frailty produced what the clinical literature terms an *inverted parentification* in a sensitive child: he absorbed early that *his* affective needs could not be brought into the room because the caregiver could not bear them. The behavioral residue is unmistakable. The subject does not tell May when he is hurt. He has not told May when he was hurt across six decades. The pattern generalizes — he does not tell *anyone* he is hurt unless physically incapable of concealment. The phrase "I'm fine, Aunt May" is, in the file, the single most-repeated utterance attributed to him outside the quip itself.

Ben Parker provided warmth without the systemic capacity to model emotional repair: he was, in the canon, a man who taught duty and patience but not how to be wounded in front of someone you love. Peter therefore inherited a moral grammar without an affective grammar. He knows what to *do* with feeling; he does not know what to do *with* the feeling itself.

**Stratum III — The peer-rejection layer (Midtown High, ages 12–17).** Chronic, daily, public invalidation by the peer-group dominant (Flash Thompson) and the female social arbiter set (Liz Allan's circle), with the home environment unable to absorb the spillover. The downstream signature is a permanent expectation of social rejection that survives, unchanged, *all* subsequent evidence of his desirability. Mary Jane Watson chose him. Felicia Hardy pursued him. Gwen Stacy loved him. The Avengers recruited him. None of this dislodges the operating assumption — visible in every internal monologue across writers — that he is, beneath whatever performance is currently working, the unwanted one. This is the durable cognitive distortion of the invalidated child: the data never updates the schema.

The composite of these three strata yields the attachment classification: **anxious-preoccupied with strong fearful-avoidant secondary features and a disorganized loading under intimacy-plus-threat conditions.** He wants closeness with an urgency that registers as charm to most observers and as alarming intensity to a few (Betty Brant noted it; Felicia Hardy weaponized it; MJ alone metabolized it). He flinches from closeness once achieved, through mechanisms he experiences as duty.

---

## 7.2 — The Bonding Sequence: How He Forms Attachment

Across every documented relationship — familial, romantic, collegial, professional — the subject runs a consistent four-phase bonding protocol. The phases are not chosen; they are reflexive.

**Phase 1: Disarming self-deprecation.** First contact involves a verbal move that lowers his own status before the other party can. Variants observed: the bumbled greeting, the spilled coffee, the joke at his own expense, the apology for existing in the doorway. With Mary Jane (ASM #42, the "face it, tiger" sequence), the subject is depicted as stammering and visibly off-balance; the pattern recurs with virtually every new significant tie. Functionally, this is preemptive self-rejection — he establishes the worst of himself first, so that subsequent acceptance is felt as real rather than as a misunderstanding awaiting correction.

**Phase 2: Acts of unsolicited service.** Within hours to days of any bond he wishes to keep, the subject performs an act of help that exceeds the situation: fixing the broken thing in the kitchen, walking someone home, staying up to help with the lab problem, building the device they mentioned needing. This is the second compensation: he establishes utility before he establishes self. The bond is anchored not in his being-loved but in his being-needed. This is also, predictably, the structural reason his relationships are unstable: utility-anchored bonds collapse the moment utility is interrupted, and his life consists of perpetual interruption.

**Phase 3: Selective disclosure of vulnerability — but only of pre-licensed material.** The subject will reveal financial difficulty, lab failure, family worry. He will not reveal the Spider-Man fact, the depth of his guilt about Ben, the recurrence of Gwen in his interior life, or his sleep state. He releases the second-tier wounds to create the impression of intimacy while withholding the first-tier wounds entirely. Most partners experience the second-tier release as full disclosure and do not register that a wall has been moved, not removed.

**Phase 4: The covert test.** Once the bond is established, the subject performs an act calculated — though not consciously — to determine whether the other party will tolerate his disappearing. He cancels. He vanishes mid-date. He fails to show. He is "called away." This is operationally indistinguishable from the genuine demands of the Spider-Man identity, and that is precisely the function: he uses the legitimate duty as a vehicle for a covert attachment test. If the partner stays, the bond deepens. If the partner leaves, the schema is confirmed, the grief is severe but expected, and the cycle resets.

This is the relational template. It is recognizable in every significant attachment in the file.

---

## 7.3 — Trust, Distrust, and the Mask Calculus

Trust, for this subject, is bifurcated along the line of mask-disclosure, and the bifurcation produces an asymmetry no observer should miss.

**Trust-as-reliability** — the assumption that another person will act consistently, keep their word, not weaponize information — he extends generously, almost recklessly. He has trusted Norman Osborn (repeatedly), Otto Octavius (repeatedly), the Black Cat after multiple betrayals, Tony Stark during Civil War, and a sequence of teammates whose behavior would have justified greater hedging. This generosity is consistent with the prosocial bias and with the underlying anxious-preoccupied need for closeness: distrust costs proximity, and proximity is the scarce resource.

**Trust-as-disclosure** — the willingness to reveal the Spider-Man identity, or the wound beneath it — he extends almost never, and when he does extend it, he does so under a specific condition: the other party has already independently inferred the truth. Mary Jane discovered the identity on her own (a fact retconned and clarified across multiple runs); the disclosure to her was a confirmation, not a revelation. Captain Stacy figured it out before death; Peter never had to choose to tell him. Otto Octavius forced the disclosure by stealing the body. The pattern of *voluntary* unprompted full-disclosure to a non-family civilian is, across canon, essentially empty.

The clinical reading: the subject does not experience disclosure as a relational gesture; he experiences it as a burden transferred. To tell someone is to make them a target, to weight them with his guilt, to introduce into their life the same vector of catastrophe that took Ben and Gwen. He is, in his own framework, *protecting* people by withholding — and the secondary gain is that withholding preserves the wall that keeps the bifurcated self-system intact (see §3, *Self-concept*).

Distrust, when it does arise, has two distinct signatures. **Tactical distrust** (assessment that a specific actor intends specific harm) is well-calibrated, evidence-responsive, and updates appropriately. **Identity-level distrust** (the schema that he is fundamentally not chooseable, that praise is misdirected, that any partner will eventually leave once they see clearly) is hermetic, evidence-resistant, and operates beneath conscious access. The first is a skill. The second is the wound.

---

## 7.4 — Betrayal: Felt and Inflicted

**Betrayal felt.** The subject's response to being betrayed by a trusted figure is, atypically, *not* primarily anger. The dominant first affect is depressive collapse and self-blame — *I should have seen it, I let this happen, this is what I get for trusting* — followed, on a delay of hours to weeks, by a contained and morally surgical anger that targets the specific act without escalating to broad revenge. The Otto/Superior aftermath is exemplary: the subject's first internal move on recovery is to inventory the damage Otto did to *his* relationships and apologize, not to pursue retribution. The Norman Osborn case is the partial exception — the post-Gwen beating of Osborn is the closest the file has to uncontained rage, and it remains, decades on, the moment the subject is depicted referring to with shame.

**Betrayal inflicted.** This is more complex and underappreciated. The subject inflicts a specific kind of betrayal on nearly every intimate partner: he withholds, he disappears, he prioritizes the mission over the promise, and he does so while loudly maintaining the relational fiction. The partners are not wrong to feel betrayed by the missed anniversaries, the bruises he cannot explain, the bank account that never recovers, the late-night absences that read as infidelity. He never intends betrayal and is consistently shocked when partners name it as such. This shock is itself diagnostic: he has so thoroughly recoded his abandonment-of-others as moral obligation that he cannot perceive its relational damage in real time. The "One More Day" sequence is the apotheosis: faced with May's death, he unilaterally trades his marriage to a metaphysical entity without consulting his wife, and he experiences this as love.

---

## 7.5 — Repair: The Mechanism and Its Limits

Repair, when the subject performs it, has a recognizable structure.

He returns. He apologizes — and his apologies are characteristically over-broad, accepting more fault than the situation requires, in a way that telegraphs the underlying self-concept (any rupture must be his fault because he is the failure-component in any system). He performs an act of restorative service, usually disproportionate to the rupture. He makes a self-deprecating joke that gives the other party permission to forgive without further extracting from him. And he does not, then or later, examine the underlying pattern that produced the rupture, because doing so would require accessing the wound the entire defensive structure exists to insulate.

The limit of his repair capacity is therefore precisely this: he can restore the *surface* of any relationship with great skill, and he cannot repair the *pattern*. Each rupture is treated as a discrete event with discrete causes — *I was late because of the Vulture, I was distracted because of Octavius, I missed the funeral because of Doom* — and the underlying constancy (he is always going to be late, distracted, missing) is never named. Partners who stay long enough begin to perceive the pattern themselves; MJ named it explicitly across the late Stern and DeFalco runs and across JMS. He listens, agrees, changes nothing structural.

There is one circumstance under which the subject performs deeper repair: when the partner threatens to leave for cause and he believes the threat. Under this condition he is capable of brief sustained behavioral modification — punctuality, presence, partial disclosure — usually lasting weeks to a few months before pressure of mission and the underlying schema reassert. The change is real but not durable, because the wound has not been touched.

---

## 7.6 — Intimacy and Dependency: The Asymmetry

The subject's intimacy pattern displays a striking asymmetry: he is willing to be *depended upon* with no upper limit, and is constitutionally incapable of *depending* in return.

He will lift the building off the partner. He will give the last dollar. He will spend the night holding the friend through the crisis. The catalogue of his generosity-under-duress is essentially the entire heroic record. What he will not do, and demonstrably has not done across sixty years, is allow himself to be the one held. When MJ has tried (across the JMS run especially), when May has tried (the post-revelation arcs), when Felicia in her better registers has tried, the subject deflects with humor, redirects to the partner's needs, or physically withdraws. *I'm fine* is, again, the signature utterance.

The clinical reading is straightforward. To depend is to expose the wound. To expose the wound is to risk the partner seeing what the subject privately believes about himself (failure, burden, the boy who let Ben die). To risk the partner seeing that is to risk the partner leaving. The defense is therefore total: he will accept no care that would require the dropping of the mask, even — *especially* — from the people who already know what is behind it.

The one partial exception is the post-Kraven sequence (DeMatteis, *Fearful Symmetry*): the burial breaks the regulation system completely, and on emergence the subject is briefly, observably *receiving* rather than only giving. The aperture closes within the arc.

---

## 7.7 — The Relational Template, Catalogued Across Targets

The template — *pursue urgently, anchor in utility, partially disclose, covertly test, sustain through service, withhold the wound, rupture through duty, repair the surface* — is observable in every long-arc relationship in the file. Brief catalog:

**Aunt May.** The foundational case. Pursuit unnecessary (the bond is given), but the rest holds: utility-anchored ("the rent, Aunt May"), partial disclosure (everything except the identity, until the late-period revelations), covert test (constant unannounced absences), sustained through service, wound withheld absolutely. Rupture-repair cycles produced by his Spider-Man absences are continuous across the entire canon, and he has never told her the full content of his guilt about Ben.

**Mary Jane Watson.** The closest thing to a successful run-through of the template, and it succeeds *because* she pre-empted the disclosure gate by knowing first. Anchored heavily in service (he is constantly building, fixing, providing); the covert test phase is essentially continuous through the marriage; the wound is partially shared but never fully metabolized in conversation. Rupture-repair cycles run on a roughly monthly tempo across the marriage canon. The "One More Day" sequence is the template's catastrophic terminal state: unable to repair, he disappears the relationship rather than allow it to witness his failure to save May.

**Gwen Stacy.** Template interrupted by death before maturation. The pursuit was urgent, the utility-anchoring conventional (academic mutual support), disclosure withheld, covert testing in progress at the time of her death — and her death therefore froze the relationship at the unresolved phase, which is structurally why she has never been mourned cleanly. The wound is the *uncompleted* template, the relationship that never had the chance to fail him in a survivable way.

**Felicia Hardy.** Template malfunction. She bypassed Phase 1 by being the pursuer; she demanded disclosure prematurely; she rejected the civilian-Peter component once disclosed (she wanted the mask, not the man), which confirmed the worst component of the underlying schema and produced years of complicated re-engagement.

**Betty Brant, Liz Allan, Carlie Cooper.** Each ran the template through Phase 3 or 4 and ruptured at the disclosure gate. In each case, the subject blamed himself entirely.

**Harry Osborn.** Same template, male-friendship register: anchored in mutual utility (roommate, lab help, financial support), partial disclosure, covert testing through absence, sustained through service, wound withheld. The Osborn complication (Harry's discovery of the identity in the context of Norman's villainy) ruptured the bond catastrophically, and the subject carried the guilt for Harry's subsequent collapse for decades.

**Johnny Storm, Daredevil, the Avengers cohort.** Same template, professional-fraternal register. With Johnny in particular, the quip-banter is the entire visible relationship surface, and beneath it the subject extends a degree of disclosure he extends to almost no civilian. The bond survives because the partner-side also runs through trauma-and-mask dynamics, allowing both parties to operate at the surface while knowing the depth is shared.

**J. Jonah Jameson.** Inverse template: a relationship the subject *cannot* rupture because it is anchored entirely in conflict, which renders it paradoxically stable. The subject's affection for Jameson, visible across all eras and explicit in JMS, depends on Jameson's failure to penetrate the disclosure gate. When Jameson eventually learns the truth in modern continuity, the relationship destabilizes precisely as the model predicts.

**Otto Octavius (Superior aftermath, Slott).** A unique case in the file: an antagonist who forcibly performed the disclosure by becoming the subject. The post-Superior relationship between the two carries a quality the subject extends to no other antagonist — a contaminated intimacy, the closeness of the one who has *been* him — and it produces relational behavior unlike any other in the catalog.

---

## 7.8 — The Template Beneath the Template

Beneath the four-phase bonding sequence and beneath the catalog of its targets is a single relational proposition the subject is, across six decades, attempting and failing to resolve:

*Can I be loved without first having saved you, and will you still be there in the morning?*

The first half is the utility-anchoring problem. The second half is the abandonment problem. He has never received, and therefore never internalized, a clean affirmative answer to either. Mary Jane came closest, and the marriage was structurally erased; May has loved him unconditionally and is held at arm's length precisely because of her fragility; Gwen was killed before the question could be answered; Felicia answered no to the first half; Ben answered yes and was then taken.

The behavioral signature of this unresolved proposition is everything in this section.
