Until it is answered — and the answer must be received, not merely offered, which is the bottleneck — the subject will continue to run the template on every new attachment, with the same compensations, the same covert tests, the same withheld wound, and the same surface-level repair. The pattern is stable. It is not, on present evidence, terminal: the prosocial scaffolding is intact, the moral coherence is unbroken, and the capacity for genuine warmth is, in defiance of the underlying schema, robust enough that partners continue to be drawn in and a meaningful fraction continue to stay.

The file's longitudinal judgment on this section: the subject is a man who has built, out of an attachment system organized around expected loss, a relational life of genuine generosity and persistent quiet starvation. He gives what he cannot receive. He repairs what he cannot examine. He is, by any honest measure, well-loved — and he does not, on the inside, know it.

— END §7 —


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

*Subject: PARKER, Peter Benjamin. Cross-reference §3 (Psychological), §4 (Psychiatric). This section maps the entire defensive architecture longitudinally — every mechanism observed across the canonical record, ranked from most mature to most primitive, with the behavioral surface each produces, the contexts in which each is deployed, and the cost each exacts. The subject's defensive system is unusually well-developed and unusually transparent: a trained observer can read his interior state from the defense currently in operation, because his repertoire is narrow, stereotyped, and escalates predictably.*

---

## 1. ARCHITECTURE OVERVIEW

The subject's defenses are organized in a tiered escalation cascade. At low affective load he operates almost entirely from the mature tier (humor, sublimation, altruism, anticipation). As load increases he descends — first into neurotic-level mechanisms (intellectualization, reaction-formation, displacement, isolation of affect), then under acute threat into immature mechanisms (somatization through the body, acting-out via violence-as-work, passive-aggressive sabotage of his civilian life), and finally under catastrophic load into the primitive tier (dissociation, splitting, denial, and — in the worst-documented episodes — fugue-like withdrawal and ideation of self-erasure framed as altruism). The cascade is unidirectional under stress and recovers in reverse under safety; the recovery is incomplete, with each major trauma episode leaving residue at the primitive tier (post-Gwen dissociation, post-Superior identity-destabilization, post-Kraven depressive imprint) that subsequent quipping and motion cannot fully discharge.

The architecture has one structural peculiarity worth foregrounding: the subject's *primary* defense (humor) and his *primary* compensation (the costumed identity) are publicly visible, audibly continuous, and physically kinetic. He cannot defend silently. This is diagnostically convenient — his defensive state can be assayed from a rooftop with binoculars — and clinically significant: a defensive system this externalized is a system that has nowhere private to retreat to. The mask is not interiority; it is *more* exteriority.

---

## 2. THE MATURE TIER

### 2.1 Humor (the quip) — primary, near-continuous, weaponized

Humor is the load-bearing defense of the entire system. It is present from Amazing Fantasy #15 in nascent form (the wrestling-circuit braggadocio), sharpened across the Romita run into the in-combat patter that has been the character's auditory signature for six decades, and elevated by Bendis (*Ultimate Spider-Man*) into near-monologue. Functionally it operates as:

- **Reaction-formation under threat.** The affect converted is *fear*; the output is its opposite — flippancy, mock-courtesy to the assailant, absurdist commentary on the assailant's costume. The conversion is most complete at the point of maximum danger. Multiple foes have explicitly noted this inversion: Kingpin ("you talk most when you are most afraid"), Octavius (who, during the Superior occupation, found he could not replicate the quip because he did not have the underlying terror to invert), Venom (who tracks the *cadence* of the quip as a tell for incoming attack timing).
- **Manic-defense against grief.** Post-loss, the quip frequency *increases* rather than decreases. After Captain Stacy's death (ASM #90) and again after Marla Jameson's, the in-combat verbal output rises measurably across the subsequent issues. The defense is anti-depressive in mechanism: speech itself is the proof of continued animation.
- **Distance regulation in non-combat.** The quip with civilians (rescued bystanders, NYPD, Jameson) operates as an intimacy-limiter. Sincere gratitude is deflected with a one-liner because acceptance of gratitude would require revising the foundational self-concept of failure. Civilians who attempt to thank him earnestly are routinely interrupted mid-sentence by a joke and a swing-away — a stereotyped exit sequence visible across thousands of pages.
- **Relational warmth-builder.** With trusted others (Human Torch, Daredevil, MJ, May), the quip becomes genuinely affectionate — softer rhythm, self-deprecating rather than other-directed, used to invite rather than repel. This is the mature face of the same mechanism and is the only form of intimacy the subject reliably tolerates.

**Cost.** The quip prevents processing. Affect that is inverted at the point of arousal is not metabolized; it is shunted. The accumulated unprocessed load is what surfaces in the depressive episodes when the quip channel is forcibly closed.

### 2.2 Sublimation — intellectual and kinetic

Sublimation operates on two channels. **Intellectual:** the lab, the formulas, the web-fluid chemistry, the iterative engineering of the web-shooters. Documented from AF #15 forward and consistent across every era. When affect is intolerable, the subject builds something. The post-Gwen issues show him in the lab; the post-Superior issues show him at Parker Industries; the post-"One More Day" issues show him retreating to invention. The product is real and useful, but the activity is defensively motivated — the engineering problem displaces the affective one. **Kinetic:** web-swinging itself. Every major artist (Ditko, Romita, McFarlane, Bagley, Ramos) has independently arrived at the same depiction — the subject's face, masked or unmasked, is *only* relaxed mid-swing. The kinetic sublimation discharges autonomic arousal that the constitutional spider-sense load and the chronic-anxiety baseline keep otherwise pinned high.

### 2.3 Altruism (defense-grade) — guilt converted to utility

In the Anna Freud taxonomy this is altruism-as-defense: the channeling of unbearable affect into compulsive other-rescuing. The mechanism is etiologically transparent — the Uncle Ben omission produced a guilt-load that could only be neutralized by the prevention of future omissions, indefinitely, without limit. The behavioral surface is the entire career. The defense is unusually salutary in effect (six decades of genuine moral action) while remaining defensively motivated in origin; this is the source of the subject's distinctive ethical signature, which is real virtue produced by an unresolved wound, both at once.

**Diagnostic marker:** the subject does not stop. He will swing on a cracked ankle, with a concussion, after forty-eight hours awake. The compulsive quality (cannot decline a save, cannot take a night off, experiences rest as moral failure) is the signature of the defense rather than the virtue.

### 2.4 Anticipation — partial, asymmetric

Anticipation is present in tactical domains (he game-plans rogues, builds counter-formulas pre-emptively, has contingency webbing for known villains) but largely *absent* in the affective domain. He does not anticipate his own grief, does not prepare for the recurrence of loss despite its statistical certainty in his life. The mechanism is split: mature in the engineering channel, undeveloped in the emotional channel. This asymmetry is itself diagnostic.

---

## 3. THE NEUROTIC TIER

### 3.1 Intellectualization

Heavy use, continuous across canon. When emotion presents he reaches for explanation — the physics of the fall, the chemistry of the toxin, the kinematics of the rescue. Post-Gwen this is most visible: the subject's internal monologue across the issues immediately following ASM #121 reverts repeatedly to the *neck-snap problem* (whether the webbing or the fall killed her), which is a *physics question* substituting for a grief question. The intellectualization is so reliable that it can be elicited on demand by any interlocutor willing to pose a technical problem — a known soft-interview technique that MJ, May, and Stark have each used at different points to manage him.

### 3.2 Reaction-formation

The quip is the principal vehicle (above), but reaction-formation also operates in his relationship to authority: the deference-then-defiance pattern with Jameson, Stark, and Fury is reaction-formation against the underlying recognition that he wants their approval. When the wanting becomes intolerable, it inverts into defiance. The Civil War repudiation of Stark reads cleanly in this frame.

### 3.3 Displacement

Affect generated in domain A is discharged in domain B. The classic instance: rage at the self (for the Ben omission, for the Gwen rescue) discharged onto villains as combat aggression. The post-Gwen beating of Osborn is the textbook example — the force applied exceeds tactical necessity by a wide margin and is recognized in the script as displacement. Lesser-scale displacements are continuous: irritation at MJ discharged as snark at Jameson, anxiety about May discharged as physical labor on the web-shooters.

### 3.4 Isolation of affect

Operates around the foundational losses. The subject can describe Uncle Ben's death in a flat factual register (to Miles Morales, to younger heroes, to MJ on rare occasion) without apparent affect, and can describe Gwen's death similarly when teaching or warning others. The affect is *not* absent; it is sequestered, retrievable only under specific conditions (anniversary dates implicit in the panels, the bridge as physical trigger, certain villains who carry associative weight). The isolation is what permits him to function operationally on dates and at locations that, in an undefended subject, would be incapacitating.

### 3.5 Undoing

Present at low intensity throughout the civilian life. Missed dates compensated for with elaborate make-up gestures; broken promises followed by disproportionate acts of service; quarrels with MJ resolved through invention of a useful object. The pattern is recognizable as undoing rather than simple repair because the compensatory gesture is *symbolic* rather than addressed to the actual injury.

### 3.6 Identification with the aggressor — partial, controlled

Visible in his combat repertoire: the subject has, over the years, absorbed and re-used techniques, postures, and even verbal patterns from defeated adversaries. The mask-and-monologue style itself is arguably an unconscious modeling on the costumed villainy of his rogues. The mechanism is held in check by the no-kill absolutism (§4) and does not reach pathological depth, but it is present and visible to any observer reading combat footage across decades.

---

## 4. THE IMMATURE TIER

### 4.1 Acting-out — channeled into work

The subject's acting-out is almost entirely sublimated into mission activity. When affect rises and the verbal channel is insufficient, he *goes out on patrol* — a behavior recognized by MJ, May, and (in the Ultimate run) Gwen as the unmistakable somatic tell of dysregulation. The patrol is partly genuine duty, partly motoric discharge. The defense becomes recognizable as acting-out rather than legitimate mission engagement when patrol duration exceeds operational necessity, when route selection becomes erratic, and when villain-engagement thresholds drop (he will pick a fight with a low-tier rogue to obtain the discharge).

### 4.2 Passive-aggressive self-sabotage ("Parker Luck")

The codified trope is, in mechanism, a passive-aggressive defense turned inward against his own civilian life. Jobs lost to lateness, relationships ruptured by unannounced disappearance, rent unpaid because the wallet was webbed to a wall — the *frequency* of these incidents across sixty years of canon exceeds any plausible attribution to external bad luck and is, on the behavioral evidence, self-generated. The mechanism: stable civilian success is incompatible with the foundational self-concept of failure; therefore stability is unconsciously dismantled the moment it threatens to consolidate. The Spider-Man identity is the convenient instrument because it provides plausible deniability — the sabotage can always be re-narrated as duty.

**Marker:** the sabotage cluster intensifies *immediately following* positive civilian developments. New job → missed shifts within two weeks. New relationship → missed dates within the month. Academic re-enrollment → withdrawn the semester. The temporal pattern is the signature.

### 4.3 Somatization

The subject's body is the bulletin board for his unprocessed affect. The chronic sleep deprivation, the chronic undereating, the willingness to operate on cracked ribs and concussions, the documented post-Kraven and post-Superior physical decompensation — these are not merely the cost of the job but somatic expression of psychic load. The enhanced healing factor masks what would otherwise be obvious wear; without it, the subject would present as a chronic-stress somatic case (gastric, dermatologic, musculoskeletal symptoms in a textbook cluster).

### 4.4 Hypochondriacal monitoring — inverted

The standard hypochondriacal defense channels anxiety into health-monitoring of the self; the subject's variant channels it into health-monitoring of *others*. He calls May after every patrol. He checks on MJ obsessively during villain breakouts. He has been depicted (Slott, Spencer) maintaining mental tallies of the locations of every attachment figure during any city-wide threat. The mechanism is the same — anxiety converted to scanning — with the target externalized in keeping with the altruistic-defense architecture.

---

## 5. THE PRIMITIVE TIER

These mechanisms surface only under catastrophic load and are the diagnostically significant ones, because they reveal what the upper tiers are holding back.

### 5.1 Dissociation

Documented across multiple major arcs. Post-Gwen (Conway, ASM #122 onward): depersonalization phenomena, derealization of the bridge environment, time-loss episodes in the immediate aftermath. Post-Kraven (DeMatteis, *Last Hunt*): the buried-alive sequence produces a sustained dissociative-depressive state that does not fully clear across the arc. Post-Superior (Slott, *Goblin Nation* and aftermath): intrusive re-experiencing of the body-occupation, depersonalization on the order of "is this hand mine," and a documented period of identity-destabilization that required external scaffolding (Anna Maria, MJ) to resolve. The dissociative capacity is moderate-to-high and is the system's emergency overflow valve.

### 5.2 Splitting — bifurcated self-system

The cardinal primitive defense in this subject and the structural engine of the entire syndrome. The Peter-self and the Spider-self are not experienced as a single person operating in two domains; they are experienced as two persons, one failed and one competent, sharing a body. The split is asymmetric in valuation (the mask is competent and valued; the face is failed and burdensome), which is the *inverse* of the typical secret-identity psychology and which generates the diagnostic "Parker Luck" pattern. The split is partial rather than global (he retains continuity of memory and moral framework across both) and so does not reach dissociative-identity severity, but it is the explanatory frame for the Civil War destabilization (collapsing the wall between the selves was experienced as collapse of the self-system itself) and for the Superior arc's particular horror (the *mask* was taken, leaving only the failed self in custody of the body).

### 5.3 Denial — narrow-band

The subject's denial is selective and high-functioning. He does not deny external reality (reality-testing is intact) but denies specific intolerable propositions: *I did not cause Ben's death by omission* (held alongside its contradiction, in compartmented form); *I am not exhausted*; *I am not afraid*; *I am fine*. The denial of fatigue and fear is continuous and is the verbal substrate of the quip. The denial of guilt is partial — he denies it operationally while affirming it morally, an unstable arrangement that is the source of the chronic depressive undercurrent.

### 5.4 Idealization / devaluation — interpersonal

Visible in the romantic pattern. Partners are idealized at onset (Betty, Gwen, MJ, Felicia, Carlie all enter the file at maximum valuation) and devalued — or rather, the *self* is devalued in relation to them — as the bond consolidates ("she deserves better than me," recurrent across writers). The devaluation is self-directed rather than partner-directed, which spares the relationships from the typical primitive-defense damage but produces the withdrawal-from-intimacy pattern that does damage by other means.

### 5.5 Altruistic self-erasure — the most dangerous mechanism in the file

The subject's most primitive defense is the *offering of the self in trade*. The pattern: faced with an intolerable loss, the subject offers something of his own — autonomy, identity, marriage, body, life — to prevent the loss. The Master Planner arc (offering his life under the machinery for May's serum). "One More Day" (offering his marriage to Mephisto for May's life). Superior (the body-trade with Octavius, which began as a victimization but contained, in its resolution, the subject's own willingness to remain erased if it would serve). The repeated structure indicates that self-erasure is not a one-off heroic gesture but a *defended position* — the offered trade discharges the unbearable affect of impending loss by converting it into action that, even if catastrophic to the self, restores agency.

The clinical significance: this is the mechanism by which the subject is most likely to be lost. He will not be killed by a villain. He will trade himself away.

---

## 6. POSITIVE COMPENSATORY STRUCTURES (NON-DEFENSIVE)

Distinct from the defenses are the compensations that are not primarily affect-management but are positive structural achievements built atop the wound.

- **The ethical code.** The no-kill absolutism, the deontological surface, the refusal of moral compromise even under personal cost. Originates defensively (killing would confirm the feared self-concept) but has become an integrated value structure that operates autonomously.
- **The mentorship instinct.** With Miles Morales, with the various Spider-people of the multiverse, with younger heroes generally. The mentorship is genuine generativity in the Eriksonian sense and is the healthiest single domain in the file. Notably, his teaching is uncharacteristically *clean* — he does not displace, does not perform, does not even quip excessively. The defenses go quiet when he is teaching.
- **The chosen-family architecture.** May, MJ, the Human Torch, Daredevil, Anna Maria. The subject has constructed across decades a small reliable kin-network that compensates for the early loss and that, despite his sabotage tendencies, has held. This is real adaptive achievement.
- **The verbal warmth in low-stakes mode.** Off-duty, off-mask, with trusted others, the subject is genuinely funny, generous, and present. The defense and the gift are the same mechanism in different registers.

---

## 7. WHAT BLOCKING EACH DEFENSE PRODUCES

For surveillance and contingency purposes the file should note the predictable consequence of forced closure of each channel:

- **Block the quip** (gag, sensory deprivation, isolation): rapid anxiety surge, somatic symptoms emerge within hours, depressive ideation within a day. Kraven's burial demonstrated this in full.
- **Block motion** (restraint, immobilization): the most acute vulnerability. Defenses collapse rapidly; rage and panic surface in alternation. The recurring torture-template villains exploit.
- **Block work/altruism** (forced inactivity, removal from mission): self-concept destabilizes within days. Documented in the rare "Peter loses his powers" arcs and in the early post-Superior recovery.
- **Block intellectualization** (deny him the engineering problem): the rumination channel opens fully and the subject decompensates into the depressive tier.
- **Force closure of the self-bifurcation** (public exposure of identity, as in Civil War): the most severe destabilization in the file short of the catastrophic-tier traumas. The architecture requires the wall.
- **Force acceptance of help/praise** (the inverse of the above): mild but persistent destabilization, deflected by quip; sustained exposure to genuine acceptance over time is, paradoxically, the single intervention most likely to produce structural change.

---

## 8. SYNTHESIS

The subject's defensive architecture is, by clinical standards, *narrow and overworked*. The repertoire is small — humor, motion, work, intellect, with a primitive substrate of splitting and altruistic self-erasure beneath — and each mechanism is used at near-maximum capacity continuously. The system is impressively functional: it has held for sixty years of canonical time under loads that have broken comparable subjects. But it is not a healthy system; it is a *successfully compensated* system, which is a different thing. The compensations have produced extraordinary moral output, durable relationships, and an ethical signature that is the most stable datum in the file. They have also prevented any genuine resolution of the foundational wound, which remains, beneath all the architecture, exactly where it was at the close of Amazing Fantasy #15: a boy who let a man walk past him, and who has been paying the bill for that omission, in installments of humor and motion and work and self, for the entire subsequent life.

The defenses are the bill being paid. They are also, in the strangest and most characteristic feature of this subject, the gift he has made of paying it.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# Longitudinal Psychological Profile

*Subject: PARKER, Peter Benjamin. Frame: clinical-developmental, decade-by-decade. The intent is to track the actual evolution of three structural variables — affect regulation, cognitive style, self-concept — across the published longitudinal record, with attention to which features were laid down early and held, which features mutated under load, and which features represent genuine repair versus mere recompensation.*

---

## I. Adolescence: the Pre-Bite Baseline and the Year of Onset (AF #15 – ASM ~#38)

### Affect regulation

At onset of the record the subject presents as a temperamentally high-reactive child in Kagan's sense: low threshold for sensory and social arousal, slow autonomic return to baseline, dominant withdrawal-coping. The Ditko-era visual grammar is consistent — averted gaze, hunched posture, the constant micro-flinch of a body anticipating contact. The home is loving but emotionally containing in only one direction: he absorbs May's worry, May does not absorb his. He has therefore been deprived, across the entire developmental window in which co-regulation is normally installed, of a caregiver who could *take in* and metabolize his distress and return it to him in tolerable form. This is the classic invalidating-environment etiology (Linehan; Chapman 2019) running not on hostility but on fragility — May's nervous system cannot afford to hear him.

The result, by fifteen, is a child whose only affect-regulation strategies are *suppression* (the closed-mouth retreat to the lab) and *cognitive distancing* (recasting peer rejection as their intellectual inferiority). Neither is functional under acute stress; both produce a brittle equilibrium.

The bite and the forty-eight-hour sequence that follows blow this equilibrium apart and install, in its place, the lifelong regulatory architecture: **humor under threat**, **motion as anxiolytic**, **work as proof-of-existence**. Within months of the wrestling-circuit episode the quip is already present — and it is already in its mature, paradoxical form, *louder* when more frightened. Clinically this is a manic defense (Klein/Winnicott) erected on the spot to manage an affect (the Ben guilt) the subject had no developmental capacity to feel directly.

### Cognitive style

Already high-g, mechanically dominant, formal-operational early. Pre-bite, the cognition is recreationally curious — the basement lab is a refuge, not a forge. Post-bite, within weeks, cognition becomes *instrumentalized*: the web-fluid, the web-shooters, the cartridges, the costume sewn on a kitchen table. Intellect is now in service of the guilt. This conversion is the single most important cognitive event of his life and it never reverses; he will never again think for pleasure without thinking for utility underneath it.

A second cognitive feature appears in this period and holds: **moral absolutism as anchor**. The "with great power" formulation is repeated to himself, not to others, with the cadence of a mantra. Mantras are cognitive prostheses for affect that cannot be sat with. The rule is load-bearing precisely because the feeling beneath it is not.

### Self-concept

Bifurcated within months of the bite, and bifurcated *asymmetrically*. The masked self is competent, audible, witnessed. The unmasked self is the boy who let Ben die. He does not yet narrate this consciously — Ditko-era thought balloons show only the surface guilt — but the structural split is already operative: he removes the mask to go home, and the change of demeanor is total. Importantly, the bifurcation in this period is not yet defended; he sometimes lets it show, sometimes envies the mask. The defenses around the split harden later.

---

## II. College and Early Twenties: Compensatory Stabilization, then the Stacy Fracture (ASM #39 – ~#150)

### Affect regulation

The Romita-era subject is visibly more *socialized*. The body has filled out, the friendships have stabilized (Harry, Gwen, MJ, Flash converted from tormentor to acquaintance), and the humor — formerly a private weapon — is now a relational asset. This is genuine development, not just compensation: he has learned, through repetition, that the quip lands, that people enjoy him, that being funny generates exactly the social acceptance the pre-bite child was denied.

But the regulation strategy is still entirely external-channel. He runs three channels in parallel: verbal (quip), kinetic (the swing — Romita and every artist since render the swing as the only setting in which his face is *unguarded*, mouth open, eyes wide, no monitoring), and labor (Bugle freelance, university coursework, heroics). When even one channel is blocked he becomes irritable; when two are blocked he becomes depressive; when all three are blocked (the Master Planner sequence, ASM #31–33) he goes to the floor of his interior and refuses to die only because someone else will.

The Captain Stacy death (ASM #90) is the first adult test of the system, and the system holds — barely — because the death can be located in a villain (Octavius) rather than in his own omission. Gwen's death (ASM #121) does not permit this evasion. The webbing-snap is *his action*, ambiguously causal, and the architecture installed against the Ben wound cannot bear a second instance of the same template at higher resolution.

The visible decompensation is immediate and severe: depressive withdrawal, the dissociative beating of Osborn (ASM #122) in which his own monologue notes that he does not recognize himself swinging, the months of avoidance of the bridge, the abortive attempts at intimacy with MJ that he sabotages before they can deepen. This is the first observable **PTSD onset** in the record — intrusive re-experiencing (the fall recurs across thought balloons for years), avoidance (the bridge), hyperarousal (already constitutional, now elevated), negative cognition about self ("I killed her" surfaces and submerges across a decade of writers).

### Cognitive style

Two changes. First, the moral absolutism *hardens into a rule* — the no-kill line, which was implicit before Gwen, becomes explicit and defended after. The cognitive function of the rule is precise: it prevents him from confirming, by killing, the worst hypothesis about himself. The deontology is psychologically motivated even where it is philosophically argued.

Second, the rumination engine ignites. Pre-Gwen, the subject thinks forward (next problem, next invention, next move). Post-Gwen, a permanent backward-facing process begins; he re-litigates failures while doing other things, and the re-litigation becomes a baseline mental activity that will run continuously, decade after decade, until the present file date.

### Self-concept

The bifurcation, formerly asymmetric, becomes **defended**. The Peter self is now actively held responsible for failure; the Spider-Man self is held responsible for action. He begins, in this period, to speak of "Spider-Man" in the third person internally — a small grammatical tell with significant clinical weight. The mask is no longer a costume, it is a *self-state*, and he is becoming aware of needing it.

---

## III. Late Twenties: the Married Adult, the Kraven Floor, the First Real Repair (ASM #150–~#400; Stern, DeFalco, Michelinie, DeMatteis era)

### Affect regulation

The marriage to MJ (Annual #21) introduces, for the first time, a relational regulator that is not purely his own production. MJ has independently identified the secret and *chosen him with it*; this is precisely the prerequisite his attachment system requires (see Section 5 of the basis: love-with-disclosure is the only love that does not feel conditional). The early-marriage period shows genuine, measurable downregulation: fewer overt depressive episodes, the humor warmer and less brittle, the rumination ongoing but periodically interruptible.

Then DeMatteis's *Kraven's Last Hunt* (1987) blocks every channel at once — buried alive, immobilized, unable to swing, unable to fight, unable to quip, unable to be seen by anyone. This is the most clinically precise stress-test in the canon, because it isolates regulation from compensation. What surfaces beneath the channels is, as predicted: depressive, ruminative, suicidally tinged, and infantile in its loneliness. He is, in the grave, the unattended child of the Forest Hills basement, with no costume and no audience and no mother who can hear him.

The post-Kraven recovery is one of the only depicted instances of *integration rather than recompensation*. He emerges shaken, talks to MJ about it (rare), and the affect runs through him rather than around him. This is the period in which the subject most closely approximates secure-base functioning. It does not last, but it happened, and it is the proof-of-concept that integration is *possible* for this subject under conditions of consistent, knowing intimate witness.

### Cognitive style

The intellectual energy in this period broadens. The lab is still the lab, but the cognition extends into ethical reflection — he begins to think about heroism rather than only execute it. The DeMatteis monologues are unusually self-aware; the Stern issues show him strategizing about *Jameson* psychologically rather than merely reacting. There is a brief window in which he is not only smart but wise.

Rumination remains chronic and the no-kill absolutism remains rigid; both are by now structural and cannot be modified by relational input alone.

### Self-concept

The bifurcation softens, modestly. Married Peter is allowed to be competent at *being a husband*, and the experience of being competent at the Peter-self thing without the mask is novel and stabilizing. He is, in this window, closer to a single integrated person than at any other point in the longitudinal record.

The clone saga (1994–96) detonates this. Whatever the in-universe metaphysics, the experiential content is: he is told that the self he just managed to integrate is *not the real self*. The integration cannot survive that, and it doesn't. The post-clone Peter is more guarded, more secretive with MJ, more reflexively self-doubting. The grammatical tic of third-personing "Spider-Man" returns.

---

## IV. Thirties: Erosion, Spiritualization, and the One-More-Day Cut (JMS era, 2001–2008)

### Affect regulation

The Straczynski period frames Peter inside a totemic-spider mythology, which the subject treats with characteristic ambivalence — intellectually skeptical, emotionally drawn, because the framework offers something his regulatory system desperately wants: *meaning for the load*. If the spider chose him, the suffering is not accident; if it is not accident, the guilt has a container.

In practice, regulation through this period is increasingly poor. May's discovery of the identity (ASM v2 #38) removes one of the foundational compartments — the lie that protected her also protected him from being fully seen at home — and the loss of that wall, paradoxically, increases his anxiety rather than relieves it, because the bifurcation is *load-bearing* (Section 5 basis: the mask separates the selves so each can function).

The Morlun arcs and *The Other* layer additional somatic violation onto an already-saturated body. The death-and-return sequence in *The Other* produces measurable post-event symptoms (intrusive imagery, identity destabilization, the brief organic-webbing/stinger phase that he experiences as not-quite-his-own-body).

Civil War (2006–07) and the public unmasking constitute the deliberate destruction of the bifurcated-self architecture by his own hand, under Stark's influence, against his actual psychological needs. The destabilization is immediate and severe; the regulation channels all run hot simultaneously (more quip, more swing, more work) and none of them suffice.

The Mephisto bargain ("One More Day," 2007) is, structurally, the largest single act of the lifelong **trade-self-for-other** pattern. Marriage — the one durable relational regulator he has ever possessed — is surrendered to prevent May's death. The clinical reading is unambiguous: under the Uncle-Ben template, any cost to self is acceptable to prevent the death of an attachment figure, and the marriage is the cost.

### Cognitive style

The cognitive style in this period shows the first signs of *fatigue*. The inventiveness is still present but more reactive than generative. The rumination has thickened into something close to a permanent low-frequency carrier wave under all other cognition. The moral absolutism wavers (Civil War temporarily breaks it before he repudiates the registration position) and the wavering itself is destabilizing, because the rule has been load-bearing for thirty published years.

### Self-concept

The bifurcation, briefly dismantled by the unmasking, is forcibly reinstalled by the Mephisto bargain — but the reinstalled version is *thinner*. He knows, at some level he cannot quite access, that he traded the marriage; the knowledge is depicted across writers as a vague, unlocatable grief he cannot name. The self-concept now contains an unresolvable item that cannot be ruminated about because it cannot be remembered. This is, in clinical analog, the structure of a dissociated traumatic memory: present in symptoms, absent from narrative.

---

## V. Late Thirties / Early Forties: Body-Theft and the After (Slott, 2010s)

### Affect regulation

The Octavius body-theft (*Superior Spider-Man*, 2012–14) is, in the subject's experiential terms, prolonged dissociative violation — consciousness suppressed inside his own body while another mind drove it. The post-event presentation (the "Peter is back" arcs and after) shows textbook complex-trauma sequelae: intrusive re-experiencing of being *inside but unable to act*, hypervigilance about loss of bodily autonomy, somatic hyperawareness, and — critically — a new and specific fear of *immobilization* that maps directly onto the file's identified pressure point (Section 5: inability to act is the single condition under which his defenses fail completely).

Regulation in this period uses the old channels but more frantically. The quipping is *faster* and *more constant* in Slott's run than at any prior point in the canon, which is precisely the predicted direction — louder defense, more saturated affect underneath. The swing is more frequent and the moments of unguarded face on the swing are *fewer*; even motion is no longer a clean refuge.

A new compensation appears: **organizational scaffolding** (Parker Industries). For the first time the subject builds an external structure that *holds him* rather than relies on his improvised solo regulation. This is, viewed charitably, a developmental step — the recognition that he cannot continue to be the sole load-bearer. Viewed less charitably, it is a manic-defense at scale, and predictably it collapses (the Hydra arc, the dissolution of the company), restoring the prior precarity which is, secretly, the only condition his self-concept can accept.

### Cognitive style

Demonstrably *less* generative in this decade than in the late-twenties peak; the cognition is more often defensive, more often back-translating Octavius's design choices in his own lab, more often catching up rather than leading. The rumination engine in this period acquires a new content domain — *what Octavius did with my body* — which compounds the older Ben/Gwen content.

The moral absolutism rehardens after the Superior period; the no-kill rule becomes, if anything, more rigid, because Octavius killed in his body and the rule is now defended against a literalized internal other.

### Self-concept

The bifurcation now has three rather than two terms — Peter, Spider-Man, and *the body that was used by someone else*. He shows, across the post-Superior arcs, a subtle but consistent estrangement from his own physical form, a slight surveillance of his own hands and reflexes. This is the somatic-mistrust signature of post-violation experience and it does not fully resolve in the published record.

---

## VI. The Present Frame: Mid-Forties Functional Equilibrium with Unhealed Cores

### Affect regulation

The current state is a **highly competent improvised regulatory system over an unresolved traumatic substrate**. The channels (quip, motion, work) operate with the smoothness of decades of practice; he can run all three under stresses that would shatter an unenhanced civilian. The system is, in DBT terms, full of distress-tolerance skills and almost devoid of emotion-regulation skills — he can survive feelings, he cannot metabolize them.

The subject has, however, accumulated genuine repair material that should not be discounted: episodic stretches of integration (the early marriage; the post-Kraven months; certain MJ-reconciliation windows), demonstrating that integration is *available* to him under conditions of consistent witnessed intimacy. The clinical implication is that the unhealed cores are not constitutional — they are unhealed because the conditions for healing have been, across six decades, intermittent rather than sustained.

### Cognitive style

Stable high-g, mechanically dominant, deontologically anchored, chronically ruminative. The cognition shows no degradation — if anything, the breadth has increased with experience — but the *signal-to-rumination ratio* has not improved across the longitudinal record. He thinks as well as he ever did; he thinks against the same unresolved content as he always has.

A late development worth noting: a slow, partially conscious *recognition of the pattern itself*. Across the most recent runs the subject occasionally observes, with grim self-amusement, that he does this — the late arrival, the secret-keeping, the trade of self for other. The metacognition is present. It has not yet, in the published record, become metabolized insight. The gap between *seeing* the pattern and *changing* it is the gap between intellectualization-as-defense and integration; he has lived in that gap for decades.

### Self-concept

The bifurcation is still the operative structure. Peter-the-failure / Spider-Man-the-competent remains the asymmetric split installed in adolescence and defended in every decade since. The Superior episode added a somatic-estrangement layer that has partially but not fully resolved. The Mephisto-shaped absence still operates as an unlocatable grief.

The single most important *stable* feature of the self-concept across all decades is the one the analytical basis correctly identified and that the longitudinal evidence overwhelmingly confirms: **the subject experiences praise as destabilizing and suffering as informative**. This is not modesty and it is not masochism. It is the signature of a self-concept organized around guilt as anchor — gratitude threatens the anchor, pain confirms it, and the regulatory system has been built, refined, and run for sixty years on that foundational orientation.

---

## VII. Trajectory Summary

| Decade | Dominant affect-regulation mode | Cognitive shift | Self-concept state |
|---|---|---|---|
| Adolescence | Suppression → quip/motion/work installed acutely | Curiosity instrumentalized to guilt | Bifurcation installed, undefended |
| Early 20s | Three-channel system stabilizes; Gwen breaks it | Rumination engine ignites; no-kill hardens | Bifurcation defended; "Spider-Man" third-personed |
| Late 20s/30s (married) | First relational co-regulation; Kraven floor; brief integration | Broadened to ethical reflection; brief wisdom window | Softened bifurcation; clone saga re-fractures |
| 30s (JMS/Civil War/OMD) | Channels run hot; mythologization attempted; bargain forecloses repair | Inventiveness fatigued; rumination becomes carrier wave | Bifurcation reinstalled thinner; unlocatable grief installed |
| Late 30s/40s (Superior+) | Frantic-channel mode; organizational scaffold attempted and collapses | Defensive cognition; rule rehardens | Tri-partite split with somatic estrangement |
| Present | Highly competent improvised regulation over unresolved substrate | Stable g; high rumination; nascent metacognition of pattern | Guilt-anchored, praise-rejecting, integration-capable but not integrated |

The longitudinal arc, read clinically rather than narratively, is **not** one of progressive deterioration nor of progressive healing. It is the arc of a fundamentally sound prosocial structure carrying an unmetabolized traumatic core through six decades, recompensating after each fresh injury, accumulating repair material in flashes that the structural conditions of his life have never let consolidate. The remarkable datum — and it must be entered into the file as such — is that across that entire arc the subject has *not* drifted ethically, has *not* exited the prosocial commitment, has *not* turned the regulation system to self-medication via substance or to other-medication via cruelty. The guilt is pathological in origin. The life built on it is not.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

## SUBJECT: PARKER, PETER BENJAMIN

*Section 4 of the Intelligence Workup. Diagnostic synthesis derived from sixty-plus years of behavioral record; provisional in the technical sense (no clinical interview has ever been conducted), but the longitudinal corpus is uncommonly dense — arguably the most extensively documented behavioral record of any single individual on the planet — and permits a degree of confidence that exceeds most lived clinical files.*

---

## 4.0 — Framing Constraints

Before any diagnostic label is applied, three caveats discipline what follows.

**First**, the subject exists inside a phenomenal frame where some of his perceptions that would be pathologized in any standard intake (precognitive threat-sense; persistent sub-auditory "hum" of incoming danger; vivid certainty of being watched or hunted) are *veridical*. The spider-sense is real. The Inheritors are real. Morlun is real. Any clinician working a standard differential would mis-code several of his Criterion A presentations as psychotic, dissociative, or paranoid; the file must therefore separate **veridical hypervigilance** (sensory truth) from **pathological hypervigilance** (autonomic loading and behavioral compensation) and grade only the latter.

**Second**, the subject's enhanced metabolism, recovery rate, and capacity to absorb physiological insult mean that the *somatic* markers normally used to triangulate psychiatric severity (weight loss, cortisol-driven inflammation, immune compromise, observable exhaustion) are masked. The body is lying about the load. The behavior is not.

**Third**, the subject's prosocial scaffolding is so robust and so longitudinally consistent that it generates a clinically misleading surface: most observers, including longtime allies, would describe him as "fine, just stressed." The dossier reads his presentation as **high-functioning concealment of a moderate-to-severe chronic burden**, not as moderate burden simpliciter.

---

## 4.1 — Primary Diagnoses (Working)

### 4.1.A — Prolonged Grief Disorder (DSM-5-TR 309.89 / ICD-11 6B42), chronic, multi-stratum, identity-organizing

This is the spine of the file. The subject meets the formal criteria — bereavement reaction persisting beyond twelve months and characterized by intense yearning, identity disruption, marked sense of disbelief, avoidance of reminders, intense emotional pain, difficulty reintegrating, emotional numbness, sense of meaninglessness, and intense loneliness — and meets them not for one loss but for a *stratigraphy* of losses each of which would, alone, satisfy threshold.

The Benjamin Parker death (subject age ~15) is the foundational stratum. It is unique in the file for three reasons: (1) it is *omissive* in causation — guilt attaches to a non-act, which is far harder to metabolize than guilt for a discrete deed because there is no bounded behavior to confess, repair, or atone for; (2) it is *secret* — the subject cannot disclose the proximate sequence (the wrestling-arena non-intervention) to the surviving caregiver without inflicting on her the precise wound he is trying to prevent; and (3) it became the founding axiom of his entire moral architecture, meaning *successful* grief work would require dismantling the scaffolding he uses to remain ethically upright. The subject is therefore structurally disincentivized from healing. This is grief that has been load-bearing for so long that it cannot be removed without collapse.

The Gwendolyne Stacy stratum (subject age early twenties) is the second great layer and the diagnostically definitive one. The bridge episode shows every marker of complicated grief: intrusive re-experiencing across decades (the falling image recurs in interior monologue under DeMatteis, Stern, Straczynski, Slott, Spencer, Wells); avoidance behavior (the subject demonstrably alters swing routes to bypass the George Washington Bridge for years at a stretch, then makes deliberate pilgrimage returns that function as exposure rituals rather than integration); identity disruption (the post-Gwen subject is canonically a different person — his marriage choices, his vocational risk tolerance, his willingness to escalate violence against Osborn, all change); and an enduring fusion of love-object with culpability that he has never severed.

Subsequent strata — Captain Stacy, Jean DeWolff, Marla Jameson, Ned Leeds, the temporary "death" of May (ASM #400), the loss of Mary Jane to retroactive cosmic dissolution (One More Day), the death of his clone-brother Ben Reilly — accrete onto the existing pattern. The clinically significant point is that **each new loss is processed through the template of the prior**, never *de novo*. He grieves Gwen by re-grieving Ben; he grieves May by pre-grieving Ben again; he grieves MJ-the-marriage by grieving Gwen again. This is the diagnostic signature of unresolved foundational grief: novel losses cannot find their own metabolic pathway.

### 4.1.B — Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (DSM-5-TR 309.81 / ICD-11 6B40), chronic, with delayed and recurrent expression

The subject meets all four DSM-5-TR symptom-cluster requirements:

- **Intrusion (Criterion B).** Recurrent involuntary memories of multiple index traumas (Ben's discovery; the bridge; the Kraven burial; the Superior body-theft). Trauma-related dreams are referenced under DeMatteis (*Soul of the Hunter*), Straczynski (*Sins Past*, *The Other*), Slott (post-Superior arcs). Dissociative reactions — moments where he loses several seconds and re-orients with the falling-Gwen image foregrounded — are explicit in canon.
- **Avoidance (Criterion C).** Route-altering around trauma sites; reluctance to discuss specific incidents (he will narrate his entire history to Mary Jane but the wrestling-arena sequence remains the latest-disclosed item across decades); avoidance of certain villains' aesthetic cues (the Goblin laugh produces measurable affect change before tactical engagement).
- **Negative alterations in cognition and mood (Criterion D).** Persistent negative self-belief ("I'm the failure, the mask is the part that works"); persistent distorted blame of self for trauma outcomes that were not under his proximate control; markedly diminished interest in non-mission activities during high-load periods; persistent inability to experience positive emotion (the canonical "swinging is the only time he smiles without effort" datum).
- **Arousal and reactivity (Criterion E).** Hypervigilance — confounded by the veridical spider-sense but exceeding it; exaggerated startle present even when the spider-sense is *not* triggered, which is the discriminating observation; sleep disturbance, chronic and severe; concentration problems under non-combat conditions despite intact and arguably superior combat-cognition; irritability under fatigue, displaced into civilian quipping that allies have learned to read as a stress index.

Criterion F (>1 month) and Criterion G (functional impairment) are abundantly met. The presentation is **chronic with delayed and recurrent expression** — meaning the diagnosis is not best fit by a single-event PTSD reading but by a cumulative-load model in which each subsequent trauma re-activates and re-consolidates prior symptom architecture. The Kraven burial in particular operates in the file as the trauma that re-encoded all earlier ones; the Superior body-theft did the same a generation later.

### 4.1.C — Affective Dysregulation, Emotion-Dysregulation-Spectrum (sub-threshold for BPD; Chapman 2019 biosocial frame)

Per Chapman (2019, *Development and Psychopathology* 31(3):1143-1156, DOI: 10.1017/S0954579419000658, PMID: 31169118), the biosocial model of borderline pathology requires the transaction of (a) constitutional emotional vulnerability/impulsivity with (b) an invalidating early environment, producing the downstream phenotype of (c) affect dysregulation, (d) interpersonal instability, and (e) self-damaging behavior. The subject's developmental record is an unusually clean fit on the *etiologic* side:

- **Constitutional emotional sensitivity.** Pre-bite Peter (AF #15 flashbacks; ASM #1 establishing material) is depicted as temperamentally shy, easily wounded, reactive — not merely introverted but affectively *thin-skinned* in a way that is consistent across every writer who has handled the pre-powers material.
- **Invalidating environment.** This is the granular fit. Peer scapegoating supplied chronic invalidation from horizontal sources (the "Puny Parker" labeling is functionally identical to the chronic invalidation Linehan describes). The home environment, while *loving*, was structurally invalidating in a subtler way: May's anxiety and fragility produced a household rule that Peter's affect could not be voiced because it might harm her — a household, in other words, that loved him but had no bandwidth to receive him. Ben's death cemented this; after Ben, the subject's *core* affective material was both unspeakable and unmetabolizable.
- **The catastrophic crystallizing event** (Ben's death and the subject's causal role) supplies the precise developmental insult Chapman's model predicts will yield maximal downstream dysregulation: an event that fuses self-concept with culpability at a developmentally pivotal age, inside an environment that cannot help process it.

The *phenotype* is present but partial, which is the key diagnostic discrimination:

- **Affect dysregulation: present.** Oscillation between manic verbal output and depressive collapse is the dominant signature.
- **Interpersonal instability under intimacy stress: present.** The pursuit-then-rupture pattern with Betty, Gwen, MJ-cycle-one, Felicia, the Black Cat resurgences, Carlie, MJ-cycle-two-post-OMD is consistent and clinically textbook.
- **Self-damaging behavior: present but channeled.** The "Parker Luck" — sabotage of employment, housing, financial stability, and the recurrent placement of body in lethal jeopardy beyond mission necessity — is the self-damaging axis. Crucially, it is *channeled* rather than *raw*: he does not cut, does not use, does not binge, does not engage in classically borderline impulsive sexuality. The danger-courting is the self-injury vector.
- **Identity diffusion: partial.** This is where the presentation falls short of full BPD. The subject's identity is *bifurcated* (Peter / Spider-Man) and the bifurcation is pathological, but it is *stable* — he is not chronically empty, he is chronically self-condemning, which is a different presentation. The fault-line is fixed; it does not migrate.
- **Frantic efforts to avoid abandonment: present but sublimated.** He does not phone-storm, he does not threaten, he does not enact classic borderline retention behavior. Instead he preemptively withdraws, which is functionally the avoidant-fearful response to the same underlying terror.
- **Recurrent suicidal behavior, gestures, threats: absent in overt form; present as ideation of self-erasure-as-relief-to-others** ("if I weren't here they'd be safe"), which is the depressive-with-PTSD presentation, not the borderline parasuicidal one.

The honest formulation: this is **sub-threshold emotion-dysregulation pathology with BPD-spectrum features in the affect-regulation and interpersonal-instability domains, scaffolded by an exceptionally strong prosocial defense system that converts what would otherwise be borderline self-injury into other-rescue.** The clinical literature would call this *adaptive sublimation* of a dysregulation core. The functional output is heroism; the substrate is the same biosocial wound Chapman describes. The quip is, in this frame, the improvised emotion-regulation skill the subject was never formally taught — equivalent in function (though not in form or efficacy) to the distress-tolerance and opposite-action skills a DBT protocol would deliberately install.

### 4.1.D — Major Depressive Disorder, Recurrent (DSM-5-TR 296.3x / ICD-11 6A71)

Episodes meeting full MDD criteria are documented in at least five longitudinal clusters: post-Gwen (Conway, ASM #122 forward); post-Kraven's-Last-Hunt (DeMatteis, *Fearful Symmetry* and immediate aftermath); post–One More Day (Brand New Day transitional material); post-Superior (Slott, 2014); and intermittently across the Spencer "Sins Rising" / "Last Remains" sequence. Each episode displays anhedonia, hopelessness, psychomotor slowing in the *Peter* presentation (the Spider-Man presentation is preserved — combat does not slow even when affect collapses, a dissociative-protective adaptation), sleep architecture disruption (always *more* disrupted than baseline, which is already disrupted), and passive suicidal ideation framed altruistically. Episodes are typically resolved by **action** (mission completion, rescue of a specific identified person) rather than by **integration**, which is the diagnostically interesting datum: his depressions remit *behaviorally* without ever being *processed*, which guarantees recurrence.

### 4.1.E — Generalized Anxiety, chronic, with somatic substrate

Layered on top of the PTSD and beneath the depressive episodes is a persistent generalized-anxiety baseline that the subject experiences as ordinary consciousness. The spider-sense alone supplies a continuous low-grade autonomic load; the subject's cognitive style (catastrophizing about loved ones' safety, especially May and MJ; pre-grieving losses that have not yet occurred; rehearsing failure scenarios while ostensibly resting) supplies the additional cognitive load that distinguishes generalized anxiety from simple physiological arousal. He worries about money. He worries about rent. He worries about being late, having failed, having been seen failing, being recognized, not being recognized, having said the wrong thing to MJ, not having said anything to MJ, May's blood pressure, May's medication, May discovering, May not discovering, the next villain, the last villain, the villain he has not yet noticed. The worry is constant and content-specific in a way that satisfies GAD criteria independent of the trauma loading.

---

## 4.2 — Comorbidity Structure and Symptom Cross-Loading

The five diagnoses above are not independent; they form a tightly coupled system in which each maintains the others.

The **PTSD** supplies the threat-priors that the **GAD** elaborates into anticipatory worry. The **prolonged grief** supplies the negative self-belief that the **MDD** episodes amplify into hopelessness. The **emotion-dysregulation substrate** supplies the affect-modulation deficit that makes both the depressive episodes and the interpersonal-instability pattern more severe than either would be alone. The **quip-and-motion regulation system** holds the whole structure in functional equilibrium between acute exacerbations — which is why removing motion (Kraven's burial), removing the mask (Civil War unmasking), or removing the body (Superior) each precipitates a decompensation cascade across multiple axes simultaneously.

The clinical analog for this kind of tightly coupled multi-diagnosis presentation is what trauma-focused literature calls **Complex PTSD with prolonged-grief and dysregulation features** — a presentation the ICD-11 captures more cleanly (6B41) than DSM-5-TR does. If forced to a single label, **Complex PTSD (ICD-11 6B41) with comorbid Prolonged Grief Disorder and recurrent Major Depressive Episodes** is the most economical formulation.

---

## 4.3 — Course Over Time

The course is **chronic, fluctuating, partially compensated, and trending toward stability through accreted competence rather than through resolution**. Six observations on trajectory:

1. **No spontaneous remission of foundational features.** The Ben-guilt and the Gwen-intrusion are present in material written across every decade from the 1960s to the present. There is no canonical period in which the subject is depicted as *not* carrying these.
2. **Episodic decompensation tied to specific stressor classes.** Each major decompensation in the file maps to one of three stressor classes: (a) immobilization/spectator-trauma (Kraven, Superior, certain Sinister Six captures), (b) attachment-figure threat or loss (post-Gwen, ASM #400, OMD bargain, Last Remains), or (c) identity-system breach (Civil War unmasking, the cloning revelations).
3. **Competence accrual.** Across runs the subject visibly improves in tactical skill, technical capability, and even in some interpersonal domains (the post-OMD subject is observably more emotionally available to MJ-as-friend than the pre-marriage subject was to MJ-as-girlfriend). The pathology has not resolved; the subject has become more skilled at carrying it. This is the realistic trajectory for chronic complex trauma in the absence of formal treatment: not healing but mastery of the load.
4. **Periodic depressive nadirs are predictable.** They follow attachment-loss and immobilization-trauma stressors with reliable latency. A surveillance file would predict them.
5. **No evidence of progression to psychosis, substance-use disorder, or antisocial drift.** The integrity of the ego across sixty years of cumulative trauma load is the single most striking longitudinal datum.
6. **Risk of catastrophic decompensation rises with simultaneous multi-axis stressor.** The file's prediction would be: if a future event combined attachment loss + immobilization + identity breach in a single sequence, the prosocial scaffolding could be exceeded. The "Last Remains" sequence approached this combination and produced his most severe documented affect collapse.

---

## 4.4 — Differential Diagnosis: What the Subject Is NOT

A surveillance-grade file is as valuable for the labels it refuses as for those it endorses. Each of the following has been considered and excluded.

### 4.4.A — Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder

The cardinal NPD feature is grandiose or vulnerable inflation of self-concept; the subject's self-concept is the inverse — chronic, stable, severe self-deprecation that functions almost as a perceptual filter. The masked persona's bravado is **anesthetic, not aggrandizing**: the quip is what allows him to act under affect-load he would otherwise be flattened by, and the persona is dropped immediately on unmasking. Praise produces deflection and discomfort, not consumption. Mirroring needs are absent; he does not require admiration to function and in fact actively distrusts it. The relational pattern is service-driven, not exploitative. NPD is excluded with confidence.

### 4.4.B — Not Antisocial Personality Disorder

Conscience is not deficient; it is hypertrophied to the point of pathology. Empathic response is robust and arguably the dominant affective channel. There is no history of childhood conduct disorder, no pattern of deceit-for-personal-gain (his secret-keeping is protective, not exploitative — a critical discrimination), no callous disregard, no impulsive aggression untethered from moral framework. The no-kill rule is preserved against extreme provocation and across decades. ASPD is excluded categorically.

### 4.4.C — Not Bipolar I or II

The mood oscillation is **reactive and context-bound**, not cyclical with autonomous episodic onset. There is no documented period of sustained elevated mood with decreased need for sleep that is *not* attributable to acute mission load. There is no grandiosity, no goal-directed activity expansion beyond baseline workaholic pattern, no pressured speech that is not better explained by the quip-as-regulation system. Sleep deprivation is chronic but voluntary/circumstantial, not driven by reduced sleep *need*. The depressive episodes are real but unipolar in structure. Bipolar spectrum is excluded.

### 4.4.D — Not Schizophrenia-Spectrum or Other Primary Psychotic

Reality testing is intact and unusually robust given the cumulative cognitive load. The unusual perceptual experience (spider-sense) is veridical, externally verifiable, and behaviorally adaptive — the inverse of the disorganizing and maladaptive nature of psychotic perception. There are no negative symptoms (avolition, alogia, blunting) outside of acute depressive episodes, and within those episodes they remit with the episode. No formal thought disorder. No delusional architecture. Excluded.

### 4.4.E — Not Dissociative Identity Disorder

The Peter / Spider-Man bifurcation is structurally a **bifurcated self-concept**, not a dissociated identity system. Both presentations share continuous autobiographical memory, continuous values, continuous skill-set, continuous voice (the quip is *more* pronounced under the mask, not categorically different). There are no time losses, no inter-identity amnesia, no third-person identity-switch experiences. The clone-saga material is in-universe literal, not dissociative; the Superior body-theft was an external imposition, not an endogenous switch. DID is excluded.

### 4.4.F — Not Obsessive-Compulsive Disorder (proper)

The compulsive responsibility-taking has *coloring* of obsessional content but fails the discriminating criteria: the content is **mood-congruent guilt** (consistent with prolonged grief and depression), not **ego-dystonic intrusion**. He does not experience the responsibility-thoughts as alien, irrational, or unwanted; he experiences them as the moral truth of his situation. There are no ritualized compulsive behaviors performed to neutralize obsessions. The patrol routines and check-on-May behaviors are mission-coherent, not ritual-coherent. OCD-proper is excluded; obsessive-compulsive *traits* are present and overlap with the prolonged-grief presentation.

### 4.4.G — Not full Borderline Personality Disorder

Discussed at length in §4.1.C above. The discrimination turns on (a) identity diffusion — bifurcated and stable, not chronically empty and migratory; (b) parasuicidal behavior — channeled through danger-courting heroism rather than overt self-injury; (c) impulsivity in cardinal domains — *absent* (no substance use, no impulsive sex, no impulsive spending beyond financial precarity which is structurally rather than impulsively caused, no impulsive interpersonal aggression); (d) frantic abandonment-avoidance — present in motivation but inverted in expression (preemptive withdrawal rather than retention behavior). Sub-threshold dysregulation-spectrum, not full BPD.

### 4.4.H — Not Adjustment Disorder

Excluded on duration and severity grounds. Adjustment disorder requires symptoms in response to identifiable stressor with onset within three months and resolution within six months of stressor termination. The subject's symptoms are chronic, multi-stressor-driven, and persist across decades without stressor termination. Excluded categorically.

### 4.4.I — Not a Hero Archetype Misread as Pathology

This is the most important differential and the one most likely to be missed by a clinician reading a sensationalized record. The subject's heroism is **not** sympt


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — SUBJECT: PARKER, P. B.

*Section 7 of the longitudinal file. All entries derived from direct observational record across the canonical run (Amazing Fantasy #15 through current publication) and cross-validated against multiple writer/artist tenures. Where a tell is era-bound, the era is noted; where it is invariant across sixty years of record, it is marked **[INVARIANT]**.*

The catalog is organized by state. Within each state: somatic tells, verbal tells, kinetic/locomotor tells, decision-habits, and predictable failure modes. Read laterally — most of the diagnostic value lies in cross-state comparison (what disappears under threat that was present at baseline; what surfaces under grief that is otherwise suppressed).

---

## 7.1 BASELINE / CALM (unmasked, low-arousal, private)

True calm in this subject is rare and almost always solitary. The published record contains perhaps a hundred clean baseline observations across six decades; the smallness of that number is itself the datum.

**Somatic.** Shoulders carried noticeably forward and slightly elevated — a chronic guarding posture that does not fully release even in sleep (depicted consistently from Romita Sr. through Pichelli). Resting respiration is shallow and high-thoracic. Hands restless: he fidgets with small objects — pen caps, lens cloths, the corner of a textbook, a camera strap — and produces, when seated, a low-amplitude bouncing of the right knee that disappears the moment he becomes aware of it. Jaw is held slightly clenched; the masseter is visibly developed in close-ups (a tell present from the Ditko era forward). Eyes scan room perimeters on entry, every time, before settling. **[INVARIANT]**

**Verbal.** Speech rate at baseline is already faster than civilian norm but coherent; sentences are full, often parenthetically nested, and self-correcting mid-clause. He thinks out loud when alone — a habit clearly established in adolescence in the basement lab and never extinguished. He narrates small operations to himself ("okay, the capacitor goes — no, the *other* one —"). When others are present, this narration converts into either murmured asides or, with sufficient comfort, the quip register.

**Kinetic.** Movement is economical and surprisingly quiet. He places objects down rather than setting them; closes doors with his back; ascends stairs two at a time without registering effort. He sits on furniture *backwards* (chairs reversed, legs over couch arms) with above-chance frequency — a long-standing tell that the body does not orient to civilian seating defaults and is always partially configured for vertical or inverted use.

**Decision-habits.** Defers small consumption decisions (what to eat, what to wear) almost without thought; deliberates intensely over expenditures above roughly thirty dollars. Will reread a technical paper four times before accepting he understands it; will accept a moral framework in one pass and then never revisit it. Procrastinates on civilian administrative tasks (rent, paperwork, replying to messages) to the very edge of consequence, then completes them in a single concentrated burst.

**Failure modes at baseline.** Boredom is poorly tolerated and converts within minutes into either work or worry — there is no idle state. Genuine leisure is unfamiliar and, when imposed (vacations, forced rest), produces restlessness, then guilt, then a manufactured reason to break the rest.

---

## 7.2 LOW-STRESS SOCIAL (civilian, daylight, no immediate threat)

**Somatic.** Posture opens slightly; the shoulders release perhaps fifteen percent. Smile is asymmetric — left side activates faster, a tell present in nearly every artist's rendering of the unmasked face. Eye contact is warm but brief; he tends to look at the bridge of the nose or the mouth rather than directly into the pupil, and breaks contact downward (rather than sideways) when transitioning to listening. Hands return to fidget patterns whenever the conversation pauses.

**Verbal.** The quip surfaces here as social lubricant rather than defense. It is gentler in this register — self-deprecating, observational, calibrated to the audience. He performs the joke for the other person's relief, not his own. With strangers he is courteous-to-deferential, with familiars warmly teasing, with children noticeably patient. Will ask three questions before volunteering one fact about himself. Pronoun usage skews to "we" and "you" rather than "I."

**Kinetic.** Light contact with familiars — a hand to a shoulder, a brief squeeze of an arm — initiated by him roughly one in four interactions, almost always as departure or arrival markers. Will adjust his pace to match a slower companion without comment. Stands slightly off-axis to interlocutors (not square-on); the masked-self combat geometry has bled into the civilian body.

**Decision-habits.** Says yes reflexively to requests for help, then privately recalculates the cost. Once committed, will not retract. Pays for things he cannot afford when in company. Routes himself to the seat with sightlines to all exits and tends to sit with his back to a wall — a hypervigilance tell that registers as ordinary preference to the untrained observer.

**Failure modes.** Self-disclosure is the bottleneck. When a conversation turns to him directly, the quip-density rises sharply (a measurable tell — joke frequency roughly doubles within sixty seconds of the topic pivoting to his interior state) and the conversation is redirected outward within two exchanges. Sustained sincere attention from another person produces visible discomfort: he looks away, scratches the back of his neck (a tell since the Lee/Ditko run), and deploys a question.

---

## 7.3 INTIMACY (romantic, deep friendship, post-coital, pre-disclosure)

**Somatic.** With the very small number of people inside the perimeter — May, MJ, latterly Anna Maria, the Human Torch in the bro register, occasionally Daredevil — the guarding partially drops. Shoulders settle. He sleeps with at least one limb in contact with the partner (cross-validated across Mantlo, DeFalco, JMS, and Slott depictions of the marriage and its analogs). With MJ specifically, his hand finds the small of her back as the default tactile resting position.

**Verbal.** Quip frequency drops below baseline — the lowest measured rate in his entire behavioral spectrum. With MJ he speaks in fragments and pet-names; with May he reverts to a slightly younger register, including childhood vocatives. He becomes capable of long silences with intimates and only with intimates; the silence is restful rather than evasive.

**Kinetic.** Forehead-to-forehead contact is the signature intimacy posture (consistent from the Stacy era through the present). Will press his lips to the top of the partner's head as a closing gesture. Carries small objects of the partner's — a hair tie on the wrist, a borrowed book — past the point of utility.

**Decision-habits and failure modes.** This is the state in which the dysregulation-core most visibly leaks. The closer the intimacy, the higher the probability of *preemptive rupture* within seventy-two hours: a missed dinner, an unexplained absence, a phone call cut off mid-sentence with a transparent excuse. The pattern is so consistent across writers that it constitutes a near-law of the subject's behavior — peak intimacy produces, within roughly three days, a Spider-Man-coded interruption. Whether the interruption is genuinely necessary or manufactured is, in the subject's own experience, indistinguishable; the spider-sense and the abandonment-anxiety speak in the same register.

**Pre-disclosure asymmetry.** With partners who do not know the secret (Betty, Liz, early Felicia, civilian relationships across the post-OMD era), the intimacy ceiling is hard and low — he cannot relax past a certain threshold and tends to terminate the relationship before it reaches the boundary. With partners who *do* know (MJ, post-revelation Felicia, Carlie briefly), the ceiling raises but the rupture pattern intensifies because the stakes of loss have risen.

---

## 7.4 MASKED-SELF OPERATIONAL (in costume, no immediate threat — patrol, transit, surveillance)

**Somatic.** The mask is an anxiolytic. Heart rate, by inference from his own monologue ("easier to breathe up here"), drops on donning. Posture inverts — under the mask he hangs from things upside down by preference, and the inverted hang is depicted across runs as his thinking posture, his eating posture, and his casual-conversation-with-other-heroes posture. The body unfolds in the costume in a way it does not unfolded.

**Verbal.** Internal monologue, when rendered (Lee, Conway, DeMatteis, Slott, Spencer), runs almost continuously and is markedly more confident than the unmasked voice. The external quip — to himself, to no one, to passing pigeons — runs in parallel and serves as both rehearsal and proprioceptive metronome.

**Kinetic.** Movement is the relaxed state. Swinging is depicted by virtually every artist of record as the only condition in which his musculature is fully released; the body in flight is loose where the body at rest is held. Pathing is non-optimal by design — he takes the long way, the higher way, the more aesthetically pleasing arc, in a way no purely tactical operator would. Familiar routes are deeply grooved: certain rooftops, certain water-tower perches, the Brooklyn Bridge pylons (despite or because of Gwen), the Daily Bugle clock, the Baxter Building setback. He returns to these locations with a regularity that would render him predictable to any sustained surveillance.

**Decision-habits.** Will divert mid-transit for a stranger in difficulty — every single time, without exception, regardless of his own mission urgency. This is so reliable it functions as a tactical vulnerability and has been exploited by villains who manufacture civilian-distress decoys. Will not pass a child crying. Will hesitate, then descend, to address an argument that looks like it could become violent. Will eat while in costume, hanging upside down, with the mask rolled up to the nose — a signature tell that has appeared across hundreds of issues.

---

## 7.5 PRE-COMBAT / SPIDER-SENSE ALERT (threat-detected, engagement imminent)

**Somatic.** The spider-sense produces a visible micro-tell: a small involuntary tilt of the head, usually to the right, milliseconds before conscious recognition. The hairs on the back of the neck are described by the subject as standing — this is depicted as literal, not metaphor. Pupils dilate. Breathing deepens and slows. Resting tension that was present at baseline *releases* — counterintuitively, the body is calmer immediately pre-combat than immediately pre-conversation.

**Verbal.** First quip is fired within two seconds of threat recognition, frequently before the opponent has registered his presence. The opener is calibrated to the opponent's vanity — names, costume choices, recent humiliations. This is not improvisation in the way it appears; he has clearly catalogued each recurring antagonist's pressure points and rehearses material.

**Decision-habits.** Engages from above and behind by strong preference. Uses webbing to immobilize *terrain* (doors, vehicles, weapons) before bodies. Will sacrifice tactical advantage to position himself between an opponent and any civilian sightline. Identifies and clears bystanders within the first eight seconds of engagement — this is automatic and precedes offensive action.

---

## 7.6 ACTIVE COMBAT (mid-fight, sustained engagement)

**Somatic.** Pain registration is depicted as delayed — injuries that would drop a civilian are noted, filed, and revisited only after the engagement ends. He bleeds without acknowledging it. Facial expression under the mask, when shown in cutaway, is *concentrated* rather than aggressive; even at peak combat intensity, the eyes are problem-solving.

**Verbal.** Quip frequency rises monotonically with danger. This is the most diagnostically loaded tell in the file. The mapping is approximately linear: at low engagement intensity, perhaps one joke per thirty seconds; at moderate intensity, one per ten; at peak (Morlun, Kraven, the worst of the Goblin engagements), continuous patter that occasionally devolves into near-glossolalia — strings of associative wordplay that have abandoned audience consideration entirely. **The patter is the regulator.** Opponents who have correctly identified this (Kingpin, Octopus, latterly Otto-with-his-memories) have learned to read joke-density as a fear gauge.

**Silence in combat is the alarm.** When the quip stops mid-fight, the subject has either (a) recognized an opponent who genuinely frightens him at the existential level, (b) become aware of a civilian casualty he could not prevent, or (c) entered the dissociative-rage state. Allies who know him (Johnny Storm explicitly, Daredevil by inference) treat the silence as an emergency signal.

**Kinetic.** Movement repertoire is enormous and reads as improvisation but is in fact a deep library of pre-figured combinations executed at speeds that compress decision and action.
