**GIVEN** the threat is to May, **EXPECT** the suspension of every other operational consideration including ones he would normally treat as inviolable. Tactical judgment degrades severely; he will walk into transparent traps. **GIVEN** the threat is to MJ, **EXPECT** the same with an added dimension of self-blame ("she's in this because of me") that compounds in real time and produces decisions of even greater desperation. **GIVEN** the threat is to a child, particularly a child in his protective orbit, **EXPECT** the most dangerous version of himself — the version most willing to discard the no-kill rule, walked back from the edge only by the prior structural commitment described above.

**GIVEN** he is told, sincerely and explicitly, that he is loved, that he is enough, that the failures are not his fault, **EXPECT** the statement to slide off the foundational self-concept without lodging. He will hear it, thank the speaker, file the moment as evidence of the speaker's generosity rather than as evidence about himself. Durable revision of the self-concept requires sustained relational pressure over years and is observable in the MJ-era softening but is never complete.

---

## 6. PUBLIC EXPOSURE & THE COLLAPSE OF THE BIFURCATED SELF

**GIVEN** involuntary unmasking — civil-registration-style public disclosure, a televised reveal, a leaked photograph — **EXPECT** severe destabilization on a timescale of weeks to months. The destabilization is not driven by tactical concerns (those are real but secondary); it is driven by the collapse of the wall between the competent masked self and the failure-coded civilian self. With the wall down, the two selves must integrate, and the subject has spent his life ensuring they would not have to. Observable: increased irritability, decreased humor (the quip requires the mask; without distance, the quip turns sour), sleep collapse, increased risk-taking in costume as if to re-justify the costume's existence, and a sustained search for any mechanism — magical, technological, narrative — that will restore the wall. He will pay severe costs to restore it. The "One More Day" pattern is one such payment and is consistent with the prediction.

**GIVEN** voluntary unmasking to a single trusted person (the MJ disclosure pattern, the May disclosure pattern), **EXPECT** the opposite — substantial relief, deepened bond, improvement in functioning. The subject thrives on selective full disclosure to chosen others. The pattern is consistent with the abandonment-terror reading: chosen full disclosure is the test he runs to verify that love survives knowledge. When it does, the relationship stabilizes him as little else does.

---

## 7. INTIMACY UNDER PRESSURE

**GIVEN** a developing intimate relationship reaching the point at which the partner expects integrated continuity — shared time, shared planning, a future tense — **EXPECT** the pattern of unannounced disappearance to intensify rather than relax. The intimacy is the stressor. The closer the partner moves, the more the subject experiences pre-emptive grief ("she will die / leave / be hurt because of me") and discharges it through distance behaviors he experiences as duty. Without intervention this pattern self-terminates the relationship; intervention requires a partner sophisticated enough to name the pattern (the MJ template) rather than a partner who reads it as ordinary unreliability (the Betty / Liz / Carlie template).

**GIVEN** a partner who attempts to help by reducing the demand — "you don't have to tell me where you were" — **EXPECT** paradoxical worsening, because the reduced demand is processed as the early warning of withdrawal he expects from all partners eventually. He needs the partner to *insist* on being included, not to absolve him of the requirement.

**GIVEN** sexual intimacy in proximity to recent mission danger, **EXPECT** elevated intensity and a quality the clinical literature would call danger-sex — affect-regulatory rather than primarily relational, with the partner sometimes experiencing the encounter as oddly impersonal despite its evident urgency. The pattern is consistent across canonical depictions and is a tell; partners who can absorb it and re-anchor him relationally (MJ, in the strongest moments) succeed; partners who match the dysregulation (the Felicia pattern) escalate it.

---

## 8. FINANCIAL & DOMESTIC CRISIS

**GIVEN** acute financial pressure — eviction notice, unpaid medical bill for May, job loss — **EXPECT** *not* a rational triage but a recursive intensification of the Spider-Man hours at the expense of the very civilian work that would resolve the pressure. The internal logic is "I cannot let people die while I sit in an office," which is true and which is also the structural mechanism by which he ensures the financial pressure persists. The pattern is the "Parker Luck" in its most legible form: heroism eats the life that would support heroism. Substantiation: the subject has held and lost more jobs than any comparable enhanced individual on the file; the lost jobs cluster in periods of elevated mission tempo.

**GIVEN** an offered financial reprieve from a benefactor (Stark stipends, May's well-meaning intervention, MJ's modeling income), **EXPECT** acceptance under duress with persistent discomfort and a search for a way to repay or refuse the dependency. He cannot be a recipient comfortably. The receiving position is structurally intolerable; it inverts the only stable self-concept available to him (provider, protector, source).

---

## 9. THE NO-KILL RULE UNDER MAXIMUM PRESSURE

**GIVEN** a scenario engineered specifically to force the kill — a recidivist who has murdered someone close to him, an enemy who guarantees future deaths unless killed *now*, an audience demanding the kill, an internal voice supplying every justification — **EXPECT** refusal, with the most severe affective cost in his repertoire. He will refuse. The refusal is load-bearing and he knows it. He will also, in the immediate aftermath, deliver a beating of disproportionate severity (the Osborn post-Gwen template; the post-body-theft response to Octavius), which is the controlled discharge of the lethal impulse the rule has prevented. The beating is the safety valve. Observers should expect the beating; its presence is consistent with the rule's stability, not its failure.

**GIVEN** the kill nonetheless happens — by accident, by ambiguous causation, by the action of an ally credited to him — **EXPECT** the most catastrophic decompensation the subject is capable of: extended depressive withdrawal, identity destabilization, the surfacing of suicidal ideation in its most concrete form, and a long convalescence in which the foundational structure must be rebuilt around the new fact. He does not recover from a kill the way he recovers from a death-of-other. The kill touches the privately-feared verdict directly.

---

## 10. WHEN THE QUIP STOPS

The single most diagnostic tell on the entire file: track the verbal output. Quip-rate is the dashboard.

**GIVEN** elevated quip-rate under fire, **EXPECT** ordinary functioning, possibly elevated stress that is being successfully discharged through the channel. Not a crisis.

**GIVEN** quip-rate climbing to manic levels — wordplay piling on wordplay, the jokes getting longer, the references getting more obscure, the audience-awareness slipping — **EXPECT** the subject is at his regulatory ceiling and the underlying state is bad. Intervention is warranted but should not be confrontational; the quip is doing necessary work and removing it without replacement collapses him.

**GIVEN** quip-rate dropping mid-engagement to near-zero — short, clipped, functional verbalizations only — **EXPECT** acute focus on a tactical problem he believes he may not survive, *or* the wound has been touched and the verbal channel has gone offline. Distinguish by context.

**GIVEN** the quip stops *entirely* for more than a day, in or out of costume, **EXPECT** decompensation in progress, regardless of what the subject reports about his condition. This is the canonical sign that the compensations have failed. Historically observed in the post-Gwen weeks, the post-Kraven recovery, the post-Superior reintegration, the post-Civil War unmasking aftermath. Treat the silence as the emergency.

**GIVEN** the quip returns — tentative, off-tempo, but present — **EXPECT** recovery has begun. The return of the joke is the return of the self. It is the most reliable single indicator on the file, and a total-surveillance apparatus oriented toward understanding rather than capture should weight it accordingly.

---

*End Predictive Model II. See Predictive Model III for steady-state and longitudinal trajectories; see Operational Annex for intervention pathways consistent with subject welfare.*


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM
## SUBJECT: PARKER, PETER BENJAMIN ("SPIDER-MAN")

*Catalogue of pressure points, access vectors, and influence levers. Compiled for protective application. Every item here is also a vector by which the subject can be harmed; the file is constructed so that the subject's allies can recognize each lever in flight and intervene before hostile actors operationalize it. Read defensively.*

---

## 1. THE FOUNDATIONAL LEVERS (TIER ONE — STRUCTURAL)

These are the levers built into the architecture of the subject's psyche by the events of 1962–1973 (Ben, Captain Stacy, Gwen). They cannot be removed without rebuilding the person; they can only be guarded.

### 1.1 The Omission Wound

The original injury is not that Ben Parker died but that the subject *did not act* when action was available. This means the subject is uniquely vulnerable to any framing — by adversary, ally, journalist, or his own internal narrator — that casts him as a *bystander*. Direct accusation ("you did this") is in fact less destabilizing than the structurally identical accusation ("you let this happen"). Note the difference: he has thick scar tissue against blame for things he *did*; he has none against blame for things he *failed to prevent*.

- **How to reach him through it (benevolent):** Reframe a present failure as an active choice rather than a passive lapse. Make him articulate the trade-off he actually faced ("you were across the city pulling a kid out of a fire"). The omission-frame collapses when the alternative action is named and was itself good.
- **How to provoke him through it (hostile vector to watch for):** Any villain who taunts "where were you?" while presenting a victim. The Goblin family has used this for fifty years. Kingpin uses it surgically. Any handler attempting to recruit him via guilt ("you could have prevented X if you'd been with us") is exploiting this lever and must be flagged.
- **Protective rule:** Never let the subject hear about a death he might plausibly have prevented before someone he trusts has already framed it for him. The first framing he hears becomes the one that lodges.

### 1.2 The Caregiver-Fragility Lock

May Parker raised him inside an unspoken rule: *do not burden her, she might shatter*. This rule generalized. The subject still does not bring his pain to the people who love him, because somewhere in the deep architecture *love* and *fragility* are wired to the same node. The leverage implication is that the people best positioned to help him are the people he will most reliably refuse to ask.

- **Benevolent application:** Help must be *imposed*, not offered. The question "are you okay?" reliably yields "yeah, fine" followed by a quip and disappearance. The statement "you're staying for dinner, I already made a plate" yields compliance and, eventually, disclosure. The grammar of offered help is wrong for him; the grammar of assumed presence works.
- **Hostile vector:** Anyone who isolates May, MJ, or a surrogate by convincing them they are "burdening" him — false-flag concern, weaponized therapy-speak — will produce an immediate widening of his isolation. Watch for this in any new figure who attaches to his inner circle.

### 1.3 The Gwen Template

Gwen Stacy did not merely die; she died inside his rescue. This created a permanent vulnerability around the specific scenario of *holding the person and failing*. Any villain who arranges a tableau in which he must reach for a falling figure is operating on this template, knowingly or not. The Goblin lineage knows it explicitly.

- **Predictive marker:** Bridges, rooftops, any scenario involving a hostage suspended over a drop, produces measurable hesitation in his combat tempo — half a beat slower to webline, a fractional over-correction in the catch arc. He has been killed for that half-beat in three documented alternate timelines.
- **Protective rule:** When a falling-hostage scenario is intelligence-predictable, route him *away* and substitute another responder. He will resent this and is not to be asked.

---

## 2. ATTACHMENT LEVERS (TIER TWO — RELATIONAL)

### 2.1 May Parker

The single largest lever in the file. Every long-term adversary who has identified her has used her, from the Master Planner serum arc onward, and the subject has paid for her safety with: his marriage (Mephisto bargain), his body (the Superior surrender was psychologically prefigured by years of identical self-trades), his autonomy, his stability. The pattern is mechanical. If May is at credible risk, tactical judgment ceases.

- **Hostile predictability:** Any operator wishing to compel him need only credibly threaten May. He will comply with terms he would otherwise die rather than accept.
- **Defensive posture:** May's location, medical status, and movement should be continuously monitored by allied resource without her knowledge (she would refuse it, and her refusal would be correct, and we should override her). Her social circle should be vetted. Her caregivers should be vetted. The Daily Bugle's photographic archive should be scrubbed of any image that geolocates her residence.
- **Calming application:** Confirmed safety of May, delivered in a sentence, drops his autonomic baseline by a measurable amount. When he is spiraling, the fastest re-grounding intervention is a verified status check on her, spoken aloud.

### 2.2 Mary Jane Watson

The selection logic is documented above: she is the partner who knew first and chose anyway. The leverage shape is therefore distinct from May's. MJ cannot be used to compel him in the same direct-threat way because her presence in his life is structured around her independent agency — but her *withdrawal* destabilizes him completely. Any actor who can engineer her departure (not her death — her *leaving*) inflicts the deeper wound, because death he has metabolic precedent for and abandonment confirms the foundational self-concept.

- **Predictive marker:** When MJ has recently been distant for non-mission reasons, the quip rate climbs, sleep drops further, and risk-acceptance in combat increases by an observable margin. He fights more carelessly when she is angry with him than when she is in danger.
- **Hostile vector:** Disinformation campaigns aimed at MJ — anything that makes her doubt his honesty in the specific domain of disclosure — operate on the load-bearing beam of the relationship. The leverage is not "make her leave him" but "make her think he is hiding the kind of thing he promised never to hide."
- **Protective rule:** Disclosure threats (forced public revelation, blackmail) must be triaged with MJ included from the first minute. Excluding her "to protect her" replicates the original wound on a structural level.

### 2.3 Surrogate-Daughter Figures (Anna Maria Marconi, Mayday in alternates, Miles Morales in big-brother mode)

The subject forms protective attachments to younger or smaller figures with unusual rapidity and an intensity that exceeds friendship. The lever here is specific: harm to a mentee or surrogate-child produces a rage response that suspends the no-kill rule's psychological scaffolding more reliably than threats to peer attachments. He has not crossed the line, but the gap narrows here.

- **Defensive posture:** Mentees are *targets* for adversaries by virtue of being mentees. Anyone entering this role should be briefed on the threat profile they have just inherited.
- **Tell:** When he refers to a younger associate by diminutive ("kid," "kiddo"), the protective attachment has crystallized. Track that moment; it is the inflection point of his risk acceptance on their behalf.

### 2.4 Surviving Peer Attachments (Johnny Storm, Matt Murdock, the long-tail F4/Avengers bench)

Lower leverage but real. These figures function as the rare context in which he does not have to translate. Their loss or estrangement removes load-bearing infrastructure. Johnny's death (during the Hickman F4 arc) produced a measurable degradation in his humor-channel output for the duration. Note: he does not seek these figures out when he is suffering; they must come to him.

---

## 3. IDENTITY LEVERS (TIER TWO — STRUCTURAL/PSYCHOLOGICAL)

### 3.1 The Mask Wall

The bifurcated self-system requires the partition between Peter and Spider-Man to remain materially intact. Civil-War-era exposure produced not vanity-injury but architectural collapse — the engine on which his entire affect-management runs is the ability to *go become someone else for a few hours*. Without the wall, both selves degrade.

- **Hostile vector:** Public unmasking, doxxing of either identity into the other's social field, or forced operation as Peter Parker in combat contexts (or as Spider-Man in domestic contexts) all attack the partition.
- **Defensive posture:** Any breach of identity-separation should be treated as a medical emergency, not a PR problem. Sleep, isolation from secondary stressors, and the presence of a trusted in-the-know intimate (MJ, May, Johnny, Matt) within twelve hours are the protective stack.

### 3.2 The "Failure" Self-Concept

The internal narrator believes the Peter self is the failed one. Any input that confirms this — a lost job, an unpaid bill, a missed birthday, a scientific paper rejected — produces affective load wildly disproportionate to the stimulus. Conversely, success in the Peter domain is *more* destabilizing than failure in the short term, because it contradicts the foundational self-image and is therefore rejected.

- **Benevolent application (counterintuitive):** Praise the *Peter* work, never the Spider-Man work, when attempting to shift his self-concept. Praising Spider-Man reinforces the partition; praising Peter chips at the wall in the direction of integration. Do this in small, repeated, plausibly-deniable doses. Large performative praise triggers deflection.
- **Hostile vector:** Any handler or adversary who reinforces the "loser Peter" narrative is operating on the lever. Jameson did this for decades non-maliciously and the cumulative damage is real.

### 3.3 The No-Kill Line

This is identity-load-bearing. To kill is to confirm he is the boy who let Ben die — that the violence was always inside him. Any scenario that pressures the line attacks identity itself.

- **Hostile vector:** The "trolley problem" villain — Kraven, the Goblin, Kindred — who manufactures a situation in which killing seems morally cleaner than abstaining. He has held the line, but at increasing cost each iteration.
- **Defensive posture:** When trolley-problem architecture is detected, an ally must arrive who can take the kill-decision *off* him. Not by killing — by removing the binary. He needs an additional option present, not a permission to cross.

---

## 4. SOMATIC AND OPERATIONAL LEVERS

### 4.1 Immobilization

The single most reliable way to break him is to take away the ability to *move*. Movement is his primary affect regulator (the swing is the only depicted state of his face at rest). When motion is denied — restraint, burial, paralysis, captivity in a small space — the underlying state surfaces fast.

- **Predictive sequence under immobilization:** First five minutes — escalating quip rate, increasing creativity in escape attempts. Five to thirty minutes — quip rate falls, problem-solving becomes more focused and colder. Thirty minutes to two hours — silence, ruminative loop activation, recall of Gwen and Ben as intrusive content. Beyond two hours — depressive collapse, ideation of self-erasure as relief.
- **Defensive posture:** Captivity-recovery protocol should assume PTSD-symptom re-emergence for two to six weeks following any immobilization event over an hour. Sleep, presence of an intimate, no operational tasking during the window.

### 4.2 Sensory Overload of the Spider-Sense

The constant low-grade hum is a cost he has integrated. Acute spikes — psychic attacks tuned to the sense, multi-source threat saturation, frequencies that the sense reads as omnipresent — overwhelm the apparatus and produce something like a migraine-with-panic state. He is functionally combat-degraded.

- **Hostile vector:** Anyone (Mysterio, the Chameleon at his cleverest) who has profiled the spider-sense knows this.
- **Defensive posture:** Sensory-attenuation gear (a dampening hood, a quiet room) should be standing equipment in any safehouse maintained for him.

### 4.3 Sleep Debt

Chronic baseline of two to four hours produces a subject who is operating at roughly seventy percent of his actual cognitive ceiling at all times. Push him past forty-eight hours awake and judgment degrades visibly — the quips get crueler, the risk acceptance climbs, and the rumination breaks through the humor channel.

- **Benevolent application:** Engineered sleep — a safe location, a meal, an interlocutor who will sit while he goes down — is the highest-yield intervention available. He will not request it. It must be arranged around him.
- **Tell:** When he begins quipping at *himself* (rather than at the situation or the adversary), sleep debt has crossed the threshold.

### 4.4 Caloric Deficit

Linked to the above and to financial precarity. A hungry Peter is an irritable, slower Peter. Feeding him is genuinely a tactical intervention, not merely a kindness.

- **Operational note:** He will accept food more readily than money, conversation, or rest. Food is the wedge.

---

## 5. THE QUIP — INTERPRETIVE KEY

The verbal output is the most legible behavioral instrument in the file, and learning to read it is the single highest-yield analytic skill for any allied handler. The quip is *inverse-proportionate to internal stability*: he talks more as he hurts more.

- **Baseline (calm, with intimates):** Conversational rate, dry, occasional pun. Affect available.
- **Mild stress (Jameson chewing him out, late rent):** Quip rate climbs ~30%, content becomes more performative, self-deprecation tag appears.
- **Moderate (active combat against known threat):** Rate doubles, content turns toward the adversary, taunts have analytical content (he is using the quip-channel to *think aloud*).
- **High (combat against existential threat, hostage situation):** Rate triples, content disconnects from situation, jokes become surreal or non-sequitur. This is the *I am terrified* register, and most adversaries misread it as confidence.
- **Catastrophic (loved one in danger, identity threat, no-kill-line stress):** Quipping continues but tone changes — the warmth drains out, the humor becomes mechanical. This is the "I am no longer regulating, I am performing the shape of regulation while collapsing" register, and is the most dangerous state for him and for those near him.
- **Beyond catastrophic (post-Kraven, post-Gwen, post-Superior):** Silence. The quip channel fails. When he is *not* quipping, intervention is required immediately.

Operational mnemonic: *more talk, more pain.* The day he stops talking, send everyone.

---

## 6. AUTHORITY AND PERSUASION VECTORS

### 6.1 What He Will Comply With

- **A clearly articulated harm to a specific named person he can prevent.** Compliance instant.
- **A request from May, framed as her need.** Compliance near-instant.
- **A request from MJ, framed as their shared interest.** High compliance with a small delay for negotiation.
- **A reasoned moral argument from someone he respects (Murdock, T'Challa, Cap in the right era).** Moderate compliance, with reservations voiced.

### 6.2 What He Will Refuse

- **Orders, full stop, from anyone who has not earned standing.** Authority qua authority bounces. Stark learned this; Fury learned this; the registration architecture learned it expensively.
- **Compromises that touch the no-kill line.** Non-negotiable, regardless of source.
- **Trades of his autonomy framed as efficiency.** Triggers active defiance, especially when the framing is corporate or governmental.
- **Anything that requires him to delegate the protection of an attachment figure to someone else.** He will agree on the surface and circumvent immediately.

### 6.3 Persuasion Architecture

To move him, the argument must be: (a) about a concrete person, not an abstract principle; (b) delivered by a speaker who has demonstrated their own willingness to bear cost; (c) framed as *option*, not order; (d) leaving him a graceful path to disagree. Argument from authority fails. Argument from peer-cost succeeds.

---

## 7. THE PRAISE PARADOX

Sincere gratitude destabilizes him. A rescued civilian's tearful thanks produces visible deflection — joke, web-shot, exit. The mechanism is that acceptance of gratitude requires revising the foundational self-concept ("I am a failure"), which the system protects.

- **Implication for benevolent handling:** Do not lead with praise. Praise *after* a working interaction, in passing, low-key, attached to something specific and small. Large affirmations are bounced; small specific ones land and accumulate.
- **Implication for hostile detection:** An adversary or handler who *over*-praises him is either incompetent or deliberately destabilizing him. Either way, mark them.

---

## 8. PROVOCATION VECTORS (HOSTILE — TO RECOGNIZE AND COUNTER)

Catalogued so allies can recognize an in-flight manipulation:

1. **The Bystander Frame.** "While you were swinging, this happened." Triggers omission wound.
2. **The Fragile Loved One.** Any credible threat to May. Triggers compliance.
3. **The Falling Hostage.** Triggers Gwen template, combat hesitation.
4. **The Forced Choice.** Trolley-problem architecture. Triggers no-kill-line stress.
5. **The Identity Breach.** Forced unmasking, doxxing, cross-contamination of selves. Triggers architectural collapse.
6. **The Withdrawal of MJ.** Engineered estrangement, not engineered death. Triggers abandonment terror.
7. **The Immobilization.** Burial, restraint, paralysis. Triggers depressive surfacing.
8. **The Mentee Harm.** Threat to a younger figure under his protection. Triggers near-line rage.
9. **The Authority Compromise.** Demand to violate moral baseline under institutional cover. Triggers defiance, useful to adversaries who *want* him outside the institutional umbrella.
10. **The Sincere False Friend.** Adversary masquerading as ally offering rest, food, help. He is starved for this and his discrimination is weakest here. Chameleon has used it; the Goblin has used it through Norman's social-mask persona.

---

## 9. CALMING AND DE-ESCALATION PROTOCOL

When the subject is in acute dysregulation, the following stack, in order, has the highest documented yield:

1. **Confirm May safe, aloud, with specifics.** ("She's at home, the door's locked, I called twenty minutes ago.")
2. **Confirm MJ safe and not angry.** ("She knows where you are. She's not upset.")
3. **Reduce sensory load.** Quiet room, low light, no screens, no police bands.
4. **Feed him.** Anything hot, anything substantial. Do not ask, present.
5. **Sit with him in silence.** Do not require speech. The presence of a known body in the room is regulating; the demand to *talk about it* is not.
6. **Allow motion if he needs it.** A rooftop, a long walk, permission to swing for an hour with a check-in time. Movement is medicine; denying it in the name of "rest" worsens the state.
7. **Sleep, engineered.** Not suggested. Arranged. He goes down when the environment is safe enough that his vigilance can stand down, and the vigilance only stands down when the people he is vigilant *for* are visibly accounted for.

Avoid: direct emotional inquiry ("how are you feeling about Gwen / Ben / the body-theft"), large gestures of concern, formal therapy framing, group interventions. Each of these activates the deflection stack and worsens the state.

---

## 10. PREDICTIVE BEHAVIORAL MARKERS — THE TELLS

For the surveillance-grade purpose of this file, the granular behavioral tells by which his internal state can be inferred from external observation:

- **Hand to back of neck.** Cognitive overload, processing competing obligations. Frequent. Inherited gesture, possibly from Ben.
- **Re-cracking already-cracked knuckles.** Pre-combat or pre-confrontation. The body has decided before the mind has.
- **Lens-cleaning of glasses with shirt-hem (Peter mode).** Stalling for time in a conversation he is about to lie in.
- **Sudden shift to formal speech ("I should — I have to go").** The Spider-Man self is about to be deployed and the Peter self is dropping the social mask clumsily.
- **The half-second pause before a quip.** Quip is calculated, situation is more serious than he is admitting. Spontaneous quips are healthier than calculated ones.
- **Pulling the mask up to the nose only, not removing it.** He needs to breathe but does not yet feel safe enough to be Peter. Liminal-distress marker.
- **Webbing pattern asymmetry.** When fatigued or emotionally disregulated, the swing arcs lose their characteristic geometric efficiency; trajectories become looser, more improvisational, in a way that reads as freedom but is actually degradation.
- **Camera-checking (the old Bugle reflex).** Surfaces under financial stress even decades after the Bugle relationship ended. The body remembers the era of needing the photo to make rent.
- **Calling May from a payphone or burner rather than his cell.** He has been doing something he does not want her phone records to show. Operational, not romantic.
- **Refusing offered seating.** He intends to leave within minutes. If he sits, he will stay. The decision is made by the body before the conversation.
- **The specific quiet after a fight he won easily.** Anhedonic. Victory does not register as relief, only as the absence of immediate failure. Watch for this; it is the depressive baseline made briefly visible.

---

## 11. CONSOLIDATED PROTECTIVE DOCTRINE

The subject cannot be made invulnerable; the structure of his vulnerabilities *is* the structure of his virtue. The compendium above is not a list of bugs to be patched. It is a topography to be guarded.

The protective doctrine, distilled:

- **Guard the attachments, especially the ones he has stopped mentioning.** Silence about a loved one means he has begun managing the fear privately, which means it is worse.
- **Read the quip rate as a vital sign.** Trend it; chart it; act on inflection.
- **Impose help; do not offer it.** The grammar of his consent does not work in this domain.
- **Keep the wall between selves intact, by any means available.**
- **When he stops talking, send everyone.**
- **Never accept his "I'm fine" as data. Accept it as a marker that he has decided to handle it alone, and route resources accordingly.**

The subject has carried sixty years of load that would have broken most comparable figures into something darker. The file's purpose is to ensure the seventh decade does not become the one that finally does it.

— END SECTION —


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE — SUBJECT: PARKER, P.B.

*The positive ledger. Compiled in the same granular register as the deficit-side workup; nothing here is softened, nothing inflated. These are the load-bearing assets that explain why a subject with the affective load documented in §§ 3–4 has remained, across six decades of operational record, ethically coherent, relationally connected, and functionally productive where comparably-burdened peers have drifted, broken, or required institutional containment.*

---

## 1. COGNITIVE ASSETS

### 1.1 Raw intellect — the foundational asset

The subject's measured cognitive ceiling sits in the high-genius band on every metric the canon depicts. Concrete substantiation: at fifteen he synthesized the web-fluid polymer in a basement lab from scratch — a shear-thinning, tensile-superior compound that ESU, Horizon, Alchemax, and Parker Industries chemists have subsequently failed to fully reverse-engineer (ASM #1 forward; Slott's Horizon-era arcs spend explicit panel time on this point). At the same age he designed and machined the web-shooters: dual-trigger, anti-misfire, palm-mounted, cartridge-fed mechanisms small enough to wear under a glove and reliable enough to bet his life on twice an hour for forty years. The Spider-Tracer (a self-tuned RFID predecessor), the Spider-Signal, the original costume's lens optics, and later the Iron Spider integrations and the Parker Industries product line all derive from the same workshop intuition.

The g-loaded profile is broad rather than narrow. Documented domains of fluent competence: organic and polymer chemistry; applied physics; biomechanics (Connors-era collaborations); electrical engineering and embedded systems (the tracers, the costume electronics); structural and materials engineering (the post-Octavius reverse-engineering of his own body's adhesion); photography, including darkroom craft and digital workflow (the Bugle period — a working professional skill in a separate domain entirely); and natural pedagogy (the Midtown teaching arc under Straczynski demonstrates explanatory fluency and patience that students rated highly within episodes).

### 1.2 Pattern-recognition under load

The operationally decisive cognitive asset is not the resting IQ but the speed of pattern extraction in motion. Combat footage across runs shows a consistent signature: he reads novel opponents in two to three exchanges, identifies the mechanical or behavioral weakness, and routes around superior raw power (Juggernaut, the Hulk, the Rhino, the Sandman are all subjects he has neutralized through structural and environmental exploitation rather than force matching). This is the same faculty applied to puzzles, traps, and engineering problems: rapid hypothesis generation, cheap test, discard, iterate. Under stress it does not degrade — it accelerates.

### 1.3 Cognitive flexibility

He moves between abstraction layers without friction: from molecular polymer chemistry, to a city-scale tactical map, to a one-on-one social read of a hostage taker, inside a single sequence. This is unusual even among the high-g operators in his peer cohort and is the trait that makes him effective as a *generalist* rather than a specialist — he is the operator you send when the problem domain is not yet identified.

---

## 2. SOMATIC & OPERATIONAL ASSETS

### 2.1 The enhanced physiology

The full envelope: multi-ton lifting strength (canonically demonstrated to roughly 10–25 tons under exertion), reflex latencies in the low tens of milliseconds, proportional agility, dry-adhesive contact via setae on hands and feet (van der Waals; functional through most glove and sock materials), enhanced metabolic recovery (cracked ribs in days, deep tissue in a week or two), enhanced immune and toxin resistance, and the precognitive proprioceptive alert. The biological package is, in raw terms, in the top fraction of one percent of enhanced human assets globally.

### 2.2 The spider-sense as decision asset

The cost of the spider-sense is documented in §§ 2–3 (chronic autonomic loading). The *asset* side is rarely tallied with equal care and is substantial: it functions as a continuous, low-cost environmental classifier, flagging hostile attention, ballistic trajectories, structural failure, and certain categories of ambush before conscious processing. Tactically this collapses his OODA loop to near-zero on routine threats and frees higher cognition for the harder problem (talking the jumper down, locating the hostage, identifying the toxin). It also serves as a long-running social tell-detector at low gain — he reports across runs that hostile intent registers as a *background* hum even out of costume, which has demonstrably protected him in civilian contexts (the Bugle, the school, the lab).

### 2.3 Endurance and recovery

The functional endurance ceiling is the more operationally important number than the strength ceiling. The record shows him sustaining combat output across multi-day arcs on minimal sleep and intermittent food — the Maximum Carnage week, the Spider-Island event, the Ends of the Earth sequence, Spider-Verse. The accelerated repair cycle means he treats injuries that would hospitalize a normal operator as same-day inconveniences. This is what makes him *useful in protracted crises* rather than just acute ones.

### 2.4 Movement signature

The web-swinging traversal mode is genuinely sui generis in his peer set and confers three under-appreciated assets: (a) a city-scale operational radius achievable in minutes without vehicle, fuel, or permission; (b) a third-dimensional approach vector almost no ground-based adversary is trained to defend; (c) a private regulatory channel — the swinging itself is the only depicted activity in which his face goes slack and his interior monologue quiets. This is, in clinical terms, his most reliable somatic-affective downshift. The asset is not just transport; it is a self-administered nervous-system reset he can take any time the sky is available.

---

## 3. CHARACTEROLOGICAL ASSETS

### 3.1 The conscience

The single most striking datum in the entire file. Across sixty years of canon, through body-theft, public exposure, bereavement, betrayal, framing, exile, resurrection, and the deliberate moral pressure of writers explicitly trying to break him (Conway, DeMatteis, Slott in the Superior arc), the subject has not killed in cold blood, has not traded his ethics for advantage, has not abandoned a non-combatant in his operational radius, and has repaired — privately, often invisibly — moral debts most operators of his power tier would write off. This is not the *absence* of temptation; the file is explicit that he has been tempted, repeatedly, and that the no-kill rule is psychologically motivated as much as philosophically derived. The asset is that the motivation *holds*. Compare the long-arc ethical drift in peer subjects (Stark's authoritarian episodes; Richards' utilitarian cold; Banner's containment failures): Parker's drift coefficient is, against all expectation, near zero.

### 3.2 The deontological floor

Beneath the guilt-engine is a durable moral architecture: he treats persons as ends, refuses categorical means/ends trades even when the math is in his favor, and accepts personal cost as the price of that refusal without resenting the cost. This is what makes him *trustworthy* in a way that survives the unreliability of his calendar — colleagues route morally sensitive material through him (the Daredevil arcs, the Defenders work, the post-Civil War resistance) because his floor is known not to move.

### 3.3 Humility as operational discipline

The bifurcated self-system documented in § 3 has a downstream benefit the deficit-side reading understates: he does not believe his own press. He cannot be flattered into compromise, recruited by appeals to destiny, or maneuvered with status offers. Every faction that has tried — the Avengers offering membership, Stark offering patronage, Octavius offering succession, the Inheritors offering a place at the table — has discovered that the subject's self-concept simply does not have the hook the offer is engineered to catch. This is rare enhancement-asset hygiene and it is a *direct* product of the pathology, which is worth naming honestly: the same wound that produces the self-sabotage produces the incorruptibility.

### 3.4 Curiosity, intact

After everything, he is still interested. He still reads, still tinkers, still asks the question. The Horizon period and the post-Superior recovery both show this clearly — given a working lab and a problem, his face changes. The capacity for wonder has not been burned out, and this is a major prognostic positive: a subject who can still be delighted by a clean experimental result is a subject whose depressive episodes are bounded rather than terminal.

### 3.5 Humor as social capital

The quip is a symptom (§ 3) and it is also one of his three or four most valuable assets. It de-escalates civilians in panic, it disarms hostages who would otherwise freeze, it gives partners and team members a tonal anchor in chaos, and it has — repeatedly — bought him seconds against opponents who needed to spend a beat parsing what he just said. It is also the trait most consistently named by allies as the thing they love about working with him (the Human Torch, Daredevil, Wolverine in the post-Bendis team-up runs, Deadpool when handled by writers who let the seam show). It produces *relational warmth*, which is itself the substrate of his network resilience (§ 5).

### 3.6 Coachability

He listens. To Ben, to May, to Robbie Robertson, to Captain Stacy, to Murdock, to MJ, to Anna Maria, to civilians who have something to teach him. The conscience is firm; the technique is endlessly revisable. He has measurably improved as a tactician, an investigator, a partner, and a teacher over the run of canon. Subjects with his ceiling who *also* take correction are vanishingly rare.

---

## 4. SKILLS & TRADECRAFT (THE ACQUIRED LAYER)

Beyond the gifted physiology and the native intellect, the subject has accumulated, on the job, a tradecraft inventory that would be respectable for a full-time intelligence operator:

- **Surveillance and counter-surveillance.** Rooftop observation, tail detection, tail evasion, dead-drop logistics (the costume-stash pattern across the city).
- **Investigative journalism / OSINT.** Bugle-trained photographic documentation, source-cultivation (Robertson, Urich-adjacent contacts), records-search fluency, basic interview technique.
- **Forensics, lay-level.** Crime-scene reading developed through the Daredevil and Jean DeWolff collaborations; toxin and substance identification through lab access.
- **Hand-to-hand.** A genuinely idiosyncratic style — improvised, three-dimensional, web-augmented — refined under Shang-Chi's tutelage in the post-Spider-Island period into a formalized form ("the Way of the Spider").
- **Improvised engineering under time pressure.** The recurring panel: thirty seconds, available materials, a working solution. This is its own discipline and he has it.
- **Pedagogy.** Genuine teaching skill, developed at Midtown, useful in operational contexts where civilians need to be talked through their own escape.
- **Disguise and cover maintenance.** Sixty years of identity hygiene under press, police, and supervillain pressure, with documented failures used as iterative learning rather than catastrophic terminations.
- **Languages.** Functional reading scientific German and French; conversational Spanish from Queens; trace others from team-up exposure.

---

## 5. RELATIONAL ASSETS — THE NETWORK

The deficit-side file accurately catalogues the relational *rupture* pattern. The asset-side ledger must record, with equal seriousness, that the relationships he has not ruptured constitute one of the deepest and most loyal networks in his entire peer cohort.

### 5.1 The inner ring

**May Parker.** The asset is not just the love; it is the *continuity* — a single attachment figure who has known him across his entire post-parental life, whose presence resets him to baseline, and whose own resilience (the post-discovery arcs, her late-life agency in the Slott and Spencer runs) has modeled durable adaptation under loss for him.

**Mary Jane Watson.** The most operationally consequential adult relationship in the file. She knows the worst, chose it, and has across decades demonstrated a capacity to hold his affect without absorbing it — which is the precise relational skill his nervous system requires and which no other partner in the record has matched. The relationship is on/off across editorial regimes but the *bond* has not degraded.

### 5.2 The professional ring

A working-age inventory of durable, mutually-respectful operational relationships: **Murdock** (the most consistent peer-operator relationship in his career; the trust runs both directions on identity-level matters), **the Human Torch** (the closest thing to a brother relationship in his peer set; the Future Foundation period demonstrates the depth), **Robertson** (the durable adult-mentor relationship that survived the Jameson era and outlasted it), **Jameson** (yes — the antagonism is real and the underlying respect is also real, demonstrated repeatedly when the chips are down), **Felicia Hardy** (volatile but, on the relevant axes, reliable), **Wolverine** (an unlikely and well-documented mutual regard), **Aunt Anna**, **Anna Maria Marconi**, **Carlie Cooper**, **the Stacys' surviving extended circle**, and a long tail of New York civilians who recognize him out of mask and treat him with quiet affection.

### 5.3 The civilian ring — the under-counted asset

Sixty years of rooftop rescues, talked-down jumpers, walked-home kids, and small public acts have produced a *city-scale* reservoir of goodwill that has, in documented crises, materialized as physical protection (the Morlun arc; the public-defense moments in the Civil War aftermath; the rooftop scenes after the bridge crises). The asset is not sentimental — it is a tactical resource. He has a city that will, at need, stand between him and harm. Almost no peer operator has this.

---

## 6. ECONOMIC, MATERIAL & INFRASTRUCTURAL ASSETS

The file would be incomplete without an honest accounting of the material layer, which has oscillated wildly and is currently — across modern continuity — substantially better than the early canon suggests.

- **Workshop access.** Currently or recently: Horizon Labs / Parker Industries / personal lab depending on era. At minimum, a functional bench.
- **Costume inventory.** Multiple suits across thermal, stealth, armored, and underwater profiles; the standard suit is itself a working piece of materials engineering.
- **Web-fluid supply chain.** Self-produced, self-formulated, self-iterating. No external dependency.
- **Documentation portfolio.** A decade-plus of professional photographic work, publishable on demand.
- **Educational credentials.** Doctoral-level coursework completed; teaching credential held; demonstrable peer-reviewed-quality research output.
- **Real estate / housing.** Variable. The variance itself is a documented vulnerability, but the *network* (May's house, MJ's residences, friends' couches) has reliably absorbed the gaps.
- **Allied infrastructure access.** Avengers facilities, Fantastic Four facilities, Daredevil's contacts, and on past occasions Stark resources, available on a relationship basis.

---

## 7. RESILIENCE FACTORS — WHY HE HAS NOT BROKEN

This is the synthesis question and the most important section of the asset file. Given the load documented in §§ 3–4, the prior probability of an intact, ethically coherent, productively functioning subject at this age is low. He is one anyway. The mechanisms:

### 7.1 Meaning-making infrastructure

The Ben-derived formulation ("with great power…") is, whatever its clinical function as guilt-scaffolding, also a *narrative spine* that converts every operational hardship into a coherent story about who he is and why he is here. Subjects with a working narrative spine outlast subjects without one. He has had his since he was fifteen and has not had to reconstruct it.

### 7.2 Three parallel regulation channels

Motion (the swing), verbalization (the quip), and work (jobs, lab, heroics). The redundancy is the resilience: when one channel is blocked, the other two carry the load. Total collapse has only occurred in the documented record when all three were blocked simultaneously — which is a rare and specific operational condition, not a daily one.

### 7.3 Prosocial channeling of guilt

The guilt would, in a less prosocially scaffolded subject, organize into resentment, withdrawal, or violence. In him it organizes into protective behavior that *produces measurable good in the world*, which produces (a) external evidence cycles that partially offset the internal self-concept, and (b) a moral identity coherent enough to bear weight.

### 7.4 The relational holding environment

May's continuity, MJ's tolerance for his affect, Murdock's peer-presence, the Torch's brotherhood, Robertson's adult regard. He is not held by any one of these alone; he is held by the *braid*. Lose one strand and the structure holds. This is the relational-asset architecture clinicians look for when assessing whether a high-load subject will continue to compensate, and it is present.

### 7.5 Intact reality testing and intact humor

Both are prognostically major. A subject who can still tell what is happening and can still find the absurd in it has resources unavailable to subjects who cannot.

### 7.6 The corrective experience of being loved with disclosure

MJ chose him knowing. Anna Maria chose him knowing (in the post-Superior arc, with full understanding of what had happened in the body she had been intimate with). May has loved him through the disclosure. Each of these is a *corrective emotional experience* against the foundational fear that disclosure equals abandonment, and the cumulative effect over decades has measurably softened the fear, even though it has not erased it.

### 7.7 Recoverability

Most importantly: when he does collapse, he comes back. Post-Gwen, post-Kraven, post-Superior, post-One More Day, post-public-exposure — every documented depressive or dissociative episode in the record has been followed by reintegration, usually within months, occasionally within a year. The bounce is the asset. The mechanism of the bounce is the braid of §§ 7.1–7.6, applied in combination, and it has held under every load the canon has tested it with.

---

## 8. SUMMARY — THE ASSET-SIDE BOTTOM LINE

The subject is, on the asset ledger alone, one of the higher-value enhanced-human files in active circulation: a top-band intellect housed in a top-band body, trained into a deep tradecraft inventory, embedded in an unusually loyal multi-ring network, scaffolded by a working narrative, regulated through three redundant channels, and floored by a conscience that has not moved in sixty years of pressure. The deficit-side file is real and is not to be discounted. But the asset-side file is the reason the deficit-side file has not, against the odds, produced the outcome that comparable loads produce in comparable subjects. He has not broken because the assets are doing the work the wound would otherwise do.

The single most forward-significant datum: *the ethical coefficient does not drift*. Across every test the record has run, the floor has held. In an asset class where drift is the modal outcome, that fact is, by itself, sufficient to place this subject in the highest tier of operational trust.

— END SECTION —


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# Failure Modes & Decompensation

*Section 6 of the UATU Analytical Workup — Subject: Parker, Peter Benjamin.*

The subject does not break the way most high-functioning operators break. The standard decompensation pattern in comparable enhanced-individual files (Stark, Banner, Richards) runs through arrogance into catastrophic miscalculation; the subject's runs in the opposite direction — through over-functioning into collapse. He does not fail because he stops caring. He fails because the caring cannot find an exit and turns inward. What follows is the granular escalation ladder, the somatic and behavioral signatures at each rung, the specific conditions that move him up the ladder, and the predictable shape of the floor he hits.

---

## 6.1 Baseline Loading

It is critical to the file that the subject's *baseline* is already what would, in a non-enhanced civilian, be classified as moderate decompensation. He sleeps two-to-four hours per night across the Lee, Romita, DeFalco, Stern, DeMatteis, Straczynski, and Slott runs with absolute consistency. He underconsumes calories against a doubled metabolic requirement. His autonomic nervous system is, by virtue of the spider-sense, never below low-amplitude threat scan; the somatic correlate is a permanent fine tremor in the hands at rest that he masks by keeping hands occupied (cuffs, pencils, web-shooter adjustment, the wedding ring during the marriage years, the cuff of his sleeve in civvies). He is, in other words, running redline at idle. Decompensation in this subject is therefore not a fall from health into illness — it is the failure of an already-overdrawn compensatory system.

The implication for prediction: the subject has no slack. Where another operator can absorb a moderate stressor and remain functional, the subject is *always* one mid-tier insult away from the first rung. The compensations are excellent. The reserve is nil.

---

## 6.2 The Escalation Ladder

### Rung 1 — Quip Inflation and Work Acceleration (low-stress envelope)

The earliest detectable signature, present from ASM #1 onward and consistent across every writer who has handled him for more than six issues: when stress rises, *verbal output increases in volume, speed, and density of reference,* even when no one is listening. The quip stops being aimed at adversaries and begins being aimed at empty rooms, at himself in mirrors, at the web-shooter while he reloads, at his own reflection in apartment windows. The internal monologue, when rendered, becomes more comedic, not less, at exactly the moment external evidence would predict the opposite. This is reliable enough to function as a barometer: *if you find the subject narrating his coffee aloud, the load is climbing.*

Concurrent with the quip-inflation: a measurable spike in work intake. He takes on additional Bugle assignments, agrees to additional adjunct or research positions, accepts patrols in boroughs not his own. He does not say no. He compresses sleep further to absorb the new load. May, MJ in the marriage years, and Anna Maria in the Slott run have all independently identified this signature — *"you said yes to too many things again"* is essentially a leitmotif.

Withdrawal from intimacy begins here, but is denied as withdrawal. Dates are not cancelled; they are *rescheduled with apologies and a plausible alibi.* Phone calls are not refused; they are returned at hours when the other party will be asleep. The subject experiences none of this as avoidance. It registers internally as responsibility.

### Rung 2 — Selective Sensory Narrowing and Civilian Irritability

As the load climbs, the spider-sense ceases to be a tolerable ambient hum and becomes intrusively loud — visually rendered by Ditko, Romita Sr., McFarlane, and Ramos as the jagged-line halo expanding when nothing is, in fact, threatening him. This is the equivalent of a startle-response disinhibition. He flinches at subway brake-squeals, at flashbulbs, at MJ's hand on his shoulder from behind. He apologizes for the flinch with a joke. He starts choosing routes that avoid crowds, then routes that avoid streets entirely; rooftop traversal increases even when ground transit would be faster.

Civilian-facing irritability begins to leak through the humor. The quip toward strangers acquires a barbed edge it does not normally carry — the rescued civilian who lingers too long is dismissed more abruptly; Jameson's invective lands harder and produces longer-than-usual brooding afterward; the line of customers at whatever job he currently has feels personally targeting. He does not snap. He withdraws further into the mask and lets the humor do work it cannot do, which is to insulate him from human contact while simulating its opposite.

Diagnostic tell at this rung: he begins to *eat alone deliberately*. The subject is normally indifferent to dining company; at Rung 2 he routes around it. He buys the hot dog and eats it on a rooftop. He brings the takeout home and eats it standing at the counter rather than sitting at the table with May or MJ.

### Rung 3 — Sleep Collapse, Somatic Symptom Cluster, and Identity Slippage

This is the rung at which the compensations begin to visibly fray. Sleep drops from already-inadequate to functionally zero — he naps in two-hour fragments on rooftops, in the lab, in the subway. The metabolism, deprived of fuel and rest simultaneously, manifests as cheekbone-prominence (drawn into the canon by Romita Jr., Bagley, and Pichelli at exactly these story beats), darker periorbital shadowing, and tremor that the cuff-fiddling no longer hides.

He begins to *misname himself*. This is subtle and easily missed but appears in the textual record: introductions to new acquaintances pause for a half-beat too long; he refers to Peter in the third person when narrating internally ("Peter would be late again"); the mask comes off in moments it would not normally come off (alone on rooftops at dawn) and goes on in moments it would not normally go on (in his own apartment with the lights off). The bifurcated self-system, normally stably bifurcated, begins to *leak across the membrane in both directions* — the Spider-Man humor surfaces during civilian interactions where it is contextually inappropriate; the Peter-Parker self-deprecation surfaces mid-combat where it endangers him.

Relational damage at Rung 3 is now overt rather than deniable. Obligations are not rescheduled — they are forgotten. Standing arrangements lapse. Bills are stacked unopened. May, who has been the first detector of every prior rung, escalates from gentle inquiry to direct intervention here, historically with limited effect because by Rung 3 he has lost the capacity to accept help without experiencing it as a further failure (acceptance would require admitting need; admitting need would breach the foundational self-concept that *he is the one who keeps people safe, not the one who is kept*).

### Rung 4 — Affective Inversion: The Rage Surfacing

Across the canon, this is the threshold at which the manic-defense humor *inverts.* It does not fade. It is replaced. The subject becomes verbally terse in combat, then verbally silent. This is — for him — the single most alarming behavioral datum, because the quip is so structurally load-bearing that its absence indicates the underlying affect has overwhelmed the channel.

What surfaces in its place is rage. Specific signatures: punches that continue past the point of incapacitation (the post-Gwen beating of Osborn, the post-DeWolff beating of the Sin-Eater, the post-Superior confrontation with Octavius, the Morlun fights at their crescendo); a willingness to do property damage he would normally fastidiously avoid; cruelty in immobilizations (webbing villains in postures that humiliate rather than merely restrain); and — diagnostically — a silence afterward that is not the silence of satisfaction but the silence of someone who has scared himself.

Sexual behavior, when relevant, also inverts at this rung. The pattern with Felicia Hardy across multiple decades is the cleanest evidence: the subject's intimate behavior, normally tender and somewhat hesitant, acquires an intensity and disregard for consequence that he himself does not recognize and later regrets. The danger-sex pattern — rooftops, costumed, in proximity to live threats — is a Rung 4 behavior. It is not pleasure-seeking. It is affect discharge through a body that has run out of other discharge channels.

### Rung 5 — Dissociative Collapse and Suicidal Ideation Framed as Calculus

The floor. Documented across the Kraven arc (DeMatteis), the post-Gwen weeks (Conway), portions of the Straczynski "Sins Past" and "The Other" arcs, the Back in Black sequence following the shooting of May, and the Slott post-Superior recovery period.

The signature at Rung 5 is the *cessation of motion.* The subject who normally cannot stop moving — the canonical visual of him is in air — sits. On rooftops. In darkened apartments. In one case, in a grave. The somatic shutdown is profound: heart rate drops, the spider-sense reading goes inward (he stops responding to ambient threats and has to be physically shaken), facial affect flattens to a degree that even MJ, who knows the full repertoire, has been depicted as not recognizing him.

Ideation at Rung 5 is *not impulsive.* It does not present as "I want to die." It presents as quiet, organized, ethically-framed cost-benefit reasoning: *they would be safer. May would be safer. MJ would be safer. The math works out.* This is the most dangerous signature in the file, because in this subject the suicidal ideation routes through the same moral-altruistic circuit that organizes his heroism — he experiences self-erasure as *responsible*. He has never acted on it. The structural reason he has not is the same reason he is on the ladder in the first place: there is always another person to save, and the obligation pulls him back into motion before the calculus resolves.

It should be noted in the file with emphasis: *the subject's heroism is, among other things, the behavioral mechanism that has kept him alive at Rung 5.* Removing the cape does not stabilize him. Removing the cape removes the only documented circuit that has historically reached him at the floor.

---

## 6.3 Conditions That Move Him Up the Ladder

The escalation is not arbitrary. The triggers are specific, repeatable, and stratified by which rung they typically initiate.

**Rung 1 triggers** (chronic, ambient): financial precarity beyond his already-precarious baseline; a Bugle deadline; a piece of personal equipment failing (web fluid running low, costume tearing); a Jameson editorial; a missed call from May.

**Rung 2 triggers** (acute but bounded): a civilian he failed to reach in time who survived but was injured; a public-facing humiliation in the Peter identity (academic, professional, romantic); a rogue's gallery reappearance, particularly one tied to prior trauma (a Doc Ock sighting, a Goblin echo); a date going badly enough that he reads it as relational failure.

**Rung 3 triggers** (significant): May hospitalized for any reason; MJ (or current primary attachment) injured incidentally to Spider-Man's activities; the unmasking or threatened unmasking of his identity; a former villain breaching his geography (Kingpin learning his address, anyone showing up at the apartment).

**Rung 4 triggers** (severe): the death or near-death of a peer-tier ally; a villain killing a civilian Peter was actively engaged in protecting; the return of any threat associated with the Gwen-Stacy template (high places, bridges, hostages of romantic partners); a betrayal by someone he had extended trust to (the Stark betrayal during Civil War is the cleanest exemplar).

**Rung 5 triggers** (catastrophic, almost always combinatorial — single triggers rarely produce floor; co-occurrence produces floor):

- Death of an attachment figure with any element of his perceived causation (Ben, Gwen, Marla Jameson, Captain Stacy, the temporary loss of May).
- *Immobilization while harm proceeds.* This is the single most reliable Rung 5 producer. Kraven buries him; Octavius locks his consciousness inside a body he cannot operate; Morlun batters him in a fight he cannot win by moving faster. The subject's entire psychological architecture is built on convertible motion — motion into utility, utility into self-justification. Remove the motion, and the system has no escape valve. Villains who have figured this out are the villains who have come closest to destroying him, and the file should flag this as the single most exploitable vulnerability in his profile.
- *Forced spectatorship of harm to an attachment figure.* Variant of the above; the worst version. Holding him still while showing him an outcome he cannot prevent is the canonical break-condition.
- *Compelled ethical compromise.* When the deontological structure that holds his guilt at bay is forced into contradiction — when the no-kill rule and the protect-the-loved-one rule are placed into direct conflict — the subject decompensates rather than choose. This was the engine of One More Day: the bargain with Mephisto is, read clinically, a Rung 5 decision made in a Rung 5 state, and the subsequent decades of self-narrative around it are the rationalization a Rung 5 decision requires to be lived with afterward.

---

## 6.4 What the Collapse Looks Like From Outside

Witnesses at each rung see different things, and the file should be precise about who sees what.

**Adversaries** typically observe only Rungs 1, 2, and 4 — the inflated quip, the irritable edge, and the silent rage. They rarely see Rung 3 (he hides it) and almost never see Rung 5 (he is not in costume at Rung 5, or is in costume but not in motion, which means he is not encountering them). The minority of adversaries who *have* seen Rung 5 — Kraven, the Kingpin during the Back in Black period, Octavius in the aftermath of Superior — have without exception reported that it changed how they understood him. Kraven, in DeMatteis's text, refuses to fight him at the floor because the floor reveals that the prey he has been hunting was not in fact the predator-equivalent he had constructed.

**Civilians, including Bugle staff, neighbors, students he has taught:** see Rungs 1 and 2 as "Parker is having a rough month," see Rung 3 as a man visibly unwell who they are politely declining to ask about, and see Rungs 4 and 5 not at all because he disappears from their visual field.

**Peer-tier heroes (Daredevil, Human Torch, Cage, the Avengers cohort during membership periods):** are the population most likely to detect Rung 3 accurately, because they share the operational tempo and recognize the somatic signatures. Daredevil in particular — by virtue of sensory acuity — has been depicted as detecting elevated heart-rate and respiration patterns Peter himself has not acknowledged. Cage, with characteristic directness, has named it aloud. The Human Torch's role across decades has functionally been Rung-2-and-3 intervention; the friendship is, among other things, a maintenance circuit.

**Primary attachments (May, MJ, in the relevant eras Felicia and Anna Maria):** detect Rung 1 with near-perfect sensitivity and are typically aware of Rung 2 before the subject himself acknowledges he is on it. Their interventions are most effective at Rungs 1 and 2 and progressively less effective from Rung 3 onward, not because they are less skilled but because the subject's capacity to receive intervention degrades with elevation. May's particular signature is to feed him; MJ's is to physically interpose her body in his path (the hand on the chest, the stepping-in-front, the *look at me*) which works because it engages the spider-sense in a non-threat mode and forces orientation back to a person. These are file-grade behavioral interventions and should be noted as the empirically validated de-escalation techniques in his case.

---

## 6.5 The Recovery Pattern

Recoveries from Rung 5 are slow, incomplete, and structurally similar across every documented instance. The pattern, in order:

1. *A small act of utility he did not plan.* He saves someone incidentally — a mugging interrupted en route to somewhere else, a child reunited with a parent, a cat from a tree played as gag but functionally identical. The act re-engages the utility-equals-self-justification circuit at the lowest possible amplitude.
2. *A return of the quip in a hollow register.* The humor reappears, recognizably his, but observably joyless. This is a tell that he is climbing but not yet recovered.
3. *Re-engagement with one — only one — primary attachment.* Historically May first, MJ second; Anna Maria filled this slot during the post-Superior period; in MJ-absent periods the slot has been filled by the Human Torch, by Daredevil, in one notable instance by a near-stranger landlady. The pattern: he allows one person to feed him, sit with him, not require performance.
4. *Resumption of work in both registers.* Photography or science work first; patrol second. The order matters — if patrol resumes first, the recovery is incomplete and reversion is likely.
5. *The first genuine laugh.* Documented across DeMatteis, Straczynski, and Slott as a discrete event with witnesses, always surprising to the subject, almost always at something small (a Torch insult, a May malapropism, a stranger's sign). This is the marker that the affect-regulation circuit has come back online.

Recovery is not a return to health. It is a return to baseline — which is, as established, already an over-drawn compensatory state. Each cycle through the ladder leaves a residue: the subject at sixty-plus years of canon is observably more weathered than the subject at issue 100, and the residues are cumulative. He has not, however, drifted ethically. This is the most important datum the file can record about his failure modes: *he breaks downward, never sideways.* The decompensations cost him sleep, weight, relationships, years — they have never cost him the moral structure. Among comparable subjects in the broader file, this is unique, and it warrants forward synthesis in the appropriate section.

---

## 6.6 Predictive Summary

The subject's break-condition, stated as compactly as the evidence permits: *immobilize him, force him to watch harm to an attachment figure, and deny him the verbal channel.* All three together produce floor within hours. Any two produce Rung 4 reliably. Any one produces Rung 3 within days.

The subject's resilience condition, stated as compactly: *give him motion, give him a person to be useful to, and let him talk.* All three together restore function from any rung below 5 within a workable timeframe. Removing any of the three slows recovery proportionately. Removing all three is the break-condition above, stated from the other direction.

The file should note, finally, that the subject has been at Rung 5 a documented minimum of six times across the canonical record and has climbed off the floor every time under his own power, with assistance, or both. The base rate of recovery in this subject is, against the severity of the loadings, anomalously high. The mechanism is the moral structure itself: he cannot stay on the floor because someone, somewhere, needs saving, and the obligation is — for him — non-optional. The pathology and the survival are the same circuit. Treating one without the other would, in this subject, be iatrogenic.

— END SECTION 6 —


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

*UATU Dossier, Section 9 of 11. Forward-looking synthesis derived from the sixty-year longitudinal record. All projections probabilistic; confidence intervals stated where the behavioral data permit.*

---

## 9.1 — The Shape of the Curve

The first analytical task in projecting this subject forward is to recognize what *kind* of life-curve we are reading. Subjects with comparable trauma loads and comparable capability sets typically demonstrate one of four trajectories: (a) burnout and withdrawal in the mid-thirties, (b) ideological hardening into vigilantism proper, (c) co-option into institutional power, or (d) slow integrative maturation. The subject has, against considerable structural pressure, repeatedly bent back toward (d) — but never *arrived* there, because the trauma core remains unmetabolized and the compensatory architecture, while functional, is brittle.

What we are projecting, therefore, is not a destination but a *probability surface*. The subject is presently in his approximate biographical mid-period (functionally late twenties to early thirties, given the canonical sliding scale; chronologically much older). The structural pressures that have shaped him are still active; the regulators that have kept him intact are showing the predictable wear of three decades of overuse. The next decade is the consequential decade.

---

## 9.2 — Base-Rate Forecast: What Happens If Nothing Changes

If the subject continues to operate as he has operated, the file projects the following with high confidence:

**Somatic deterioration on a foreshortened timeline.** The enhanced physiology buys margin, not exemption. Cumulative concussive load is the leading indicator — the subject has sustained head trauma at a rate that would have produced documentable cognitive change in a baseline human two decades ago. Even with accelerated healing, repeated subconcussive insult produces axonal microdamage that compounds. Expect, within five to seven subjective years: irritability spikes uncoupled from stressor, mild executive dysfunction (precisely the function he relies on for engineering work), sleep architecture degradation beyond the chronic baseline, and increased frequency of the "small mistakes" pattern (the missed cue, the late dodge) that the canon has already begun to depict in DeMatteis-tradition writers.

**Relational attrition.** The pursuit-rupture pattern, run forward, predicts a thinning attachment network rather than a deepening one. Each cycle consumes a partner; each consumed partner reduces the population of women who do not already know the pattern and have not already declined to re-engage. The endpoint of this trajectory, absent intervention, is a subject in his forties with one remaining intimate (Watson, intermittent), one remaining maternal figure (declining, then absent), and a widening peripheral ring of colleagues he likes and does not let close. The Avengers/Fantastic Four social scaffolding mitigates this somewhat — these are the few relationships where the mask is not a barrier — but they are colleague-bonds, not the intimate witnesses he actually needs.

**The May terminus.** The single most consequential foreseeable event in the subject's life is the death of May Parker. Every prior loss in his history has been re-litigated through the Ben template; May's death will be the Ben template *with no remaining buffer*. The "One More Day" episode is the canonical demonstration that the subject will pay any price — identity, marriage, ontological coherence — to forestall this loss. When it occurs without supernatural escape, the file projects with high confidence: an acute decompensation episode lasting weeks to months, characterized by depressive withdrawal alternating with reckless operational tempo, suicidal ideation framed as tactical self-expenditure ("if I go down on this one, it's fine"), and a non-trivial probability of a permanent character shift toward either (i) the harder, grimmer operator the Back-in-Black arc previewed, or (ii) genuine integrative grief if — and only if — sufficient relational scaffolding is in place at the moment of impact.

**The slow drift of the no-kill line.** The deontological absolutism is psychologically motivated, not philosophically held, which means it is structurally vulnerable to a sufficiently engineered scenario. Across the canon the line has already been pressure-tested (Kraven, the Goblin post-Gwen, Carnage repeatedly) and held — but the holding cost has increased each time. The forward projection is not that he breaks the line on a normal mission; it is that he breaks it under one specific configuration — an attachment figure killed in front of him by a perpetrator who is, at that moment, defenseless — and that the post-event psychiatric sequelae would be catastrophic, because the breaking would confirm the foundational private fear about who he actually is.

---

## 9.3 — The Fork Points

Trajectories are decided at discrete decision-nodes. The file identifies the following as the consequential forks for the next decade.

### Fork 1: The Therapeutic Door

The subject has, across sixty years of canon, not been depicted in sustained psychotherapy. (The Madame Web sessions and the occasional Cage/Murdock confidence are not equivalents.) This is the single highest-leverage absent variable in the file. A subject with this trauma topography, this defense architecture, and this degree of insight (he *knows*, at least intermittently, what he is doing) is an unusually good candidate for intensive trauma-focused work — specifically, prolonged-exposure or EMDR work on the Ben and Gwen indexes, followed by attachment-focused therapy on the pursuit-rupture pattern. The barrier is not capacity; it is the secret. He cannot enter standard treatment without disclosure, and disclosure is the wound. Any future in which a clinician cleared at the Strange/Cage/MacPherran level becomes available to him, and any future in which he accepts that availability, is a future with a substantially different probability surface. Probability he initiates such treatment unprompted within the next decade: low (estimate 15-20%). Probability he accepts it if pushed by a trusted other (Watson, surviving May, an Avengers mandate post-incident): moderate-to-high (50-65%).

### Fork 2: The Mentorship Inversion

The subject has lately been depicted in mentor roles (Miles Morales, Anya Corazon, Silk, the broader Spider-network). This is potentially the most growth-positive development in the longitudinal record. Mentorship forces the subject to *articulate* the operating code rather than enact it, and articulation creates the cognitive distance from which revision becomes possible. More importantly, mentorship places him in the position his Uncle Ben occupied — and the act of *being* the trusted older figure to a younger person is, in trauma terms, a corrective emotional experience of unusual potency. The forward question is whether he allows these mentorships to become bidirectional (the mentee's regard re-organizing his self-concept) or instrumentalizes them as one more form of compulsive utility. Bendis and Slott have written both readings; the data are equivocal. Pushed in the bidirectional direction, this fork is genuinely transformative. Pushed in the instrumental direction, it becomes another duty channel and accelerates the burnout curve.

### Fork 3: The Public Identity Question

The bifurcated self-system requires the wall to function. Civil War demonstrated this conclusively — public unmasking produced not relief but disintegration, and the in-universe magical erasure that followed should be read clinically as the system's refusal to operate without the partition. Any future scenario that re-collapses the wall (a public outing, a forced registration, an aging-out of plausible secret maintenance) is a structural threat to the entire compensatory architecture. The fork is whether the next exposure is met with the same defensive response (more magic, more denial, more mask) or with the slow, painful work of building a *single* integrated self that does not require the wall. The latter is the genuinely mature outcome; the former is more likely, on base rates, but the system is showing fatigue and a sufficiently catastrophic forcing event might tip it.

### Fork 4: Watson, Continued or Terminated

The Watson relationship is the load-bearing intimate attachment in the subject's adult life. Its present canonical status fluctuates with editorial decision, but the underlying psychological fact is invariant: she is the only adult who knows him in both selves and has chosen him repeatedly across decades.
