The fork point is not whether they reconcile in any given storyline; it is whether the subject ever does the work necessary to stop *needing* the rupture-distance regulation that has defined the relationship's pattern. If Watson remains accessible and he does that work, the integrative trajectory becomes substantially more probable. If she becomes permanently inaccessible (death, definitive departure), the file projects a significant regression — a return to the serial-pursuit pattern with progressively younger partners, which is a classic late-thirties trauma-subject signature and is consistent with what we see in comparable longitudinal cases.

### Fork 5: The Institutional Capture Question

The subject has been recruited into the Avengers, the Future Foundation, Horizon Labs, Parker Industries, and (catastrophically) the Stark orbit during Civil War. Each institutional embedding has ended, usually badly. The forward question is whether he ever accepts a stable institutional role that provides what his life structurally lacks — material security, peer accountability, hierarchical limits on his self-expenditure — without that role compromising the moral autonomy that is, in the file's judgment, the single most valuable thing about him. The Parker Industries arc is the cautionary case: he got the security and lost the orientation. The Avengers embedding is the more promising case: peers who can both deploy him and refuse to deploy him. The fork is whether the next institutional offer comes from a structure that can hold him without instrumentalizing him. The file's prior is pessimistic; institutions that can do this are rare.

### Fork 6: The Parentage Question

If the subject becomes a parent (the Mayday-Parker future is one canonical instantiation; the Renew Your Vows continuity is another), the entire psychological architecture is reorganized around a new attachment whose loss would be definitionally unsurvivable. This is the highest-stakes fork on the surface. The file's read is counterintuitive: parentage may be *protective* rather than destabilizing for this specific subject, because the parental role is the one duty configuration that the guilt-organized altruism scaffolding is structurally optimized for, and because the corrective effect of receiving unconditional love from a child may be the single intervention powerful enough to revise the foundational failure-self. The Mayday continuity supports this reading; the subject is depicted as more integrated, less quip-shielded, more present. The risk vector is the inverse — a child harmed on his watch would produce a decompensation beyond any prior modeled scenario, and the file cannot project his survival of it.

---

## 9.4 — What Pushes Toward Growth

The growth trajectory requires, in approximate order of leverage:

**A reliable witness.** Someone who knows both selves, holds the knowledge without flinching, and refuses to accept the failure-self valuation. Watson has historically played this role intermittently; a clinician could; a fully integrated mentee in adulthood might. The mechanism is corrective re-evaluation — every time someone who knows the worst stays, the foundational equation (love is contingent on undisclosed worth) loses a small amount of credibility. Twenty years of this, and the equation degrades. He is not a subject who responds to insight; he is a subject who responds to longitudinal evidence.

**Permission to rest.** The operating code makes rest morally suspect, which means the subject cannot grant himself rest without external authorization. A trusted figure — peer, mentor, partner, institution — who explicitly tells him to stand down, repeatedly, in a frame he cannot rationalize away, can do work that he cannot do for himself. The Avengers structure has occasionally produced this; the Watson relationship at its best does; the Murdock and Cage friendships have flashes of it.

**A loss that is not his fault, processed in real time with support.** This is the most difficult intervention to engineer because it cannot be engineered — it must occur naturally and be met by sufficient scaffolding. But the underlying trauma logic requires it: the foundational equation (loss = my failure) can only be revised by repeated experience of loss that demonstrably is not his failure, witnessed by trusted others who name it as such while he is in the acute window. May's death, if it occurs in a moment of relational density rather than isolation, is the candidate event. If it occurs in isolation, it accelerates the catastrophe trajectory instead.

**Reduction in operational tempo.** Even a 30% reduction in mission load — through institutional support, through partnership with the Spider-network distributing the geographical responsibility, through a deliberate stand-down period — produces measurable benefit on the indices that matter (sleep, intimate availability, somatic recovery). The subject will resist this intensely; the resistance is itself diagnostic and predictable.

**Articulation of the operating code, repeatedly, in mentorship.** Each time he explains the "with great power" formulation to a younger operator, he hears it from outside. Sufficient repetitions, and the formulation becomes available for revision — specifically, available for the addition of the clauses it has always lacked ("and also the responsibility to remain whole enough to continue," "and also the responsibility to allow others to share the load," "and also the responsibility not to confuse penance with duty"). This is the slow path and the most promising one.

---

## 9.5 — What Pushes Toward Catastrophe

The catastrophe trajectory requires, in approximate order of impact:

**Isolation at the moment of major loss.** May's death — or Watson's, or a mentee's — occurring while the subject is operationally isolated, relationally thinned, and sleep-deprived, is the file's worst-case forcing scenario. The combination removes every regulator simultaneously. Probability of severe decompensation in this configuration: very high.

**A successful provocation across the no-kill line.** A villain with the patience and intelligence to engineer the specific scenario described in 9.2 — an attachment figure killed in front of him by a defenseless perpetrator — would produce, on breaking the line, a psychiatric outcome the file cannot project with confidence other than to note it would be severe and possibly permanent. Several extant villains have this capability profile (the Goblin most obviously, Kraven retrospectively, Octavius). The line has held for sixty years; the holding is not guaranteed.

**Institutional weaponization.** A repeat of the Civil War dynamic — a trusted institutional figure successfully instrumentalizes the guilt scaffolding to enlist him in a morally compromised project, which he then must extract himself from at enormous cost — is a recurring vulnerability. The subject's resistance to authority is real but late-firing; he tends to comply, then defect, and the defection cycle is destructive each time. A second instance of this dynamic with a less benign institutional actor than Stark would be considerably worse.

**Chronic-pain or somatic-disability onset.** If the cumulative injury load produces a permanent disability — even a partial one — that removes the swing/motion regulator from the affect-management toolkit, the system loses one of its three primary channels. The file's read is that he could survive losing the quip channel (he has periodically) and could survive losing the work channel (he has periodically), but losing the motion channel removes the one consistently depicted source of unalloyed pleasure in his life, and that loss has no compensatory pathway in the current architecture.

**A second body-theft or identity-violation event.** The Superior episode produced documentable post-event symptoms. A second such violation, particularly one involving an attachment figure or a moral compromise enacted in his body, would compound rather than habituate. The subject does not desensitize to identity violation; he sensitizes.

**Watson's permanent departure without resolution.** As covered in Fork 4. The regression vector here is well-mapped in comparable longitudinal subjects and the file projects it with reasonable confidence.

---

## 9.6 — The Open Questions

The file identifies the following as the questions that cannot be answered from the present record and that will determine the next decade.

1. **Will he ever speak the Ben sequence aloud, to a witness, in full?** The forty-eight-hour AF #15 sequence has been re-narrated by him internally across sixty years and has been alluded to in conversation, but the file cannot locate an instance of him telling another person the *full* sequence — the wrestling money, the deliberate non-intervention, the specificity of the choice. Until he does this, the wound remains encapsulated. Whether the encapsulation ever breaks is the determinative question.

2. **Does he have a child?** The probability surface bifurcates sharply at this node.

3. **What happens at May's death?** The single most consequential foreseeable event; the surrounding configuration determines everything.

4. **Does the no-kill line hold?** Sixty years of evidence say yes; the structural analysis says it is conditionally vulnerable.

5. **Is there a clinician?** The single highest-leverage absent variable.

6. **Does Watson stay?** Editorial variable in canon; psychological variable in the subject.

7. **Does he ever stop being late?** This is the trivial-seeming question that is actually a proxy for the whole architecture. The lateness is the distance-regulation; the lateness is the self-sabotage; the lateness is the secret. The day he is on time, repeatedly, to ordinary commitments, is the day the architecture has genuinely changed. The file does not project this day within the next decade with any confidence, but watches for it as the leading indicator.

---

## 9.7 — Forward Synthesis

The subject is, on every comparison the file can construct, an outlier in the salutary direction. Subjects with this trauma load typically do not retain ethical coherence; subjects with this operational tempo typically do not retain relational warmth; subjects with this defensive architecture typically harden into something colder than what he has remained. The persistence of the prosocial scaffolding across six decades, under conditions that have broken every comparable subject the file can index, is the central datum and the basis for the file's cautious optimism.

The caution is not rhetorical. The architecture is brittle. The regulators are tired. The next decade will deliver, with near certainty, at least one of the forcing events itemized above, and possibly several. Whether he survives those events as the subject this file has been tracking — recognizably ethical, recognizably warm, recognizably *himself* — depends less on his own resources, which are mostly exhausted, than on the relational and institutional scaffolding present at the moment of impact.

The forward recommendation is therefore not addressed to the subject. It is addressed to the people around him. The single most important intervention is presence — sustained, witnessed, non-instrumental presence by people who know both selves. Everything else follows from that, and nothing meaningful is achieved without it.

The subject has, for sixty years, been the person who arrived in time for everyone else. The trajectory question, ultimately, is whether anyone arrives in time for him.

— END SECTION 9 —
